**Phase 1F вАФ Strict 3-Click Lateral Alignment** *(вЬЕ IMPLEMENTED 2026-05-26)*

**Motivation.** Phase 1B/1C committed the straight wall on click 2 with its axis (centerline) coinciding with the user-picked AвЖТB line. Result: when the user clicks two endpoints of an underlay line intending to align a wall with it, the line ends up cutting the wall in half вАФ the user has no way to tell the tool *which side* of AвЖТB the wall should sit on. Industry tools (Revit "Location Line", AutoCAD Architecture "Justification") solve this with a 3-click affordance or a post-pick edge selector. Phase 1F adopts the 3-click variant: the third click is the lateral side pick, made mandatory so no wall ships without an explicit alignment.

**FSM extension.** `straight` kind now: `idle вЖТ awaitingStart вЖТ awaitingEnd вЖТ awaitingAlignment вЖТ commit вЖТ awaitingStart` (continuous chain). Click 1 stores `startPoint`, click 2 stores `endPoint` (no commit yet), click 3 commits with a lateral offset computed from the click position relative to the AвЖТB line. Polyline + curved kinds are **unchanged** вАФ only `straight` enters `awaitingAlignment`. After every commit the tool resets to `awaitingStart`, so click 1 of the next wall is unambiguously a NEW wall (no risk of the next click being mistaken for the previous wall's alignment).

**Offset math** *(pure, `computeWallAlignmentOffset` in `wall-completion.ts`)*.

```
d   = end - start                  (axis vector, canvas world units)
n   = (-dy, dx) / |d|              (CCW 90¬∞ perpendicular = "left" of AвЖТB)
cross = dx*(Cy-Ay) - dy*(Cx-Ax)    (sign tells which side C is on)
sign  = cross > 0 ? +1 : -1        (cross == 0 вЖТ zero offset, centered)
offset = sign * (thicknessMm/2) * mmToSceneUnits(sceneUnits) * n
```

`offset` is added to BOTH `params.start` AND `params.end` before building the entity. The resulting wall has the edge AWAY from C sitting exactly on the original AвЖТB click line, with the body extending TOWARD C. This matches the user expectation: "click right вЖТ left edge on line; click left вЖТ right edge on line."

**Files modified.**

- [x] `hooks/drawing/wall-completion.ts` вАФ `buildDefaultWallParams` gains optional `alignmentPoint?: Point2D | null` (5th arg). Thickness is resolved upfront (DNA preset or override) so the offset path can use it; existing callers without alignment get the legacy centered behaviour. New exported pure function `computeWallAlignmentOffset()` вАФ testable in isolation. `completeWallFromTwoClicks` mirrors the new optional arg.
- [x] `hooks/drawing/useWallTool.ts` вАФ `WallToolPhase` union gains `'awaitingAlignment'`. Straight-kind click pipeline: click 2 transitions to `awaitingAlignment` (stores `endPoint`) instead of committing; click 3 calls `commitStraightFromState(s, s.endPoint, point)` with the alignment point as the third arg. `commitStraightFromState` signature gains the optional alignment arg and forwards it to `buildDefaultWallParams`. Preview-store effect surfaces `endPoint` to the store ONLY during `straight + awaitingAlignment` (every other phase/kind keeps it null). Status text adds `tools.wall.statusAlignment`. `isAwaitingAlignment` boolean added to the hook return.
- [x] `bim/walls/wall-preview-store.ts` вАФ `WallPreviewState` gains `endPoint: Point2D | null`. `EMPTY`, `set()` deep-equality guard, and snapshot deep-copy extended.
- [x] `hooks/drawing/wall-preview-helpers.ts` вАФ `generateWallPreview` detects `preview.endPoint` (only set in `awaitingAlignment`) and renders the wall from `start вЖТ endPoint` with the live cursor as the alignment point. Outside of `awaitingAlignment` the legacy rubber-band preview (`start вЖТ cursor`) is unchanged. `makeWallFootprintGhost` accepts an optional `alignmentPoint` and forwards it to `buildDefaultWallParams`.
- [x] Dynamic Input contract вАФ `commit-wall` submitted at `awaitingEnd` BYPASSES alignment and commits centered (precision path; explicit coords leave no room for half-thickness ambiguity). Submitted at `awaitingAlignment` it is treated as the alignment side pick. Manual mouse-click users still get the strict 3-click flow.
- [x] i18n вАФ `tools.wall.statusAlignment` added to `dxf-viewer-shell.json` (el + en).
- [x] Tests Jest вАФ `useWallTool.test.tsx`: 13 tests (was 10) вАФ phase transition `awaitingEnd вЖТ awaitingAlignment`, click 3 commits with +Y / -Y / +X-axis offsets, zero-length retry from `awaitingAlignment`, status text key, overrides flow with 3 clicks. `wall-completion.test.ts`: 9 new tests for `computeWallAlignmentOffset` (colinear / degenerate / +Y / -Y / diagonal / sceneUnits='m') + `buildDefaultWallParams` alignment integration (back-compat default / DNA-thickness shift / override-thickness shift). Pre-existing wall-completion `scene-unit m` test corrected to match the SSoT spec (height/thickness stay in mm вАФ boundary conversion lives in `computeWallGeometry`).
- [x] Companion hotfix вАФ `bim/walls/wall-trims.ts` `processPair` had a unit-mismatch bug exposed by Phase 1F: `JOIN_THRESHOLD_MM` (200 mm) and `thickness/2` were used directly while `lenA`/`lenB` are in canvas world units. In meter-based scenes this inflated `epsA` (40√Ч larger), spuriously classified every wall pair as a junction, and emitted a bevel of ~2 m that `applyAxisBevels` then interpreted as canvas units вЖТ start of the new wall shifted by 40% of its length. Fix: multiply `halfA`, `halfB`, and `joinThreshold` by `mmToSceneUnits(params.sceneUnits)`. 19 existing `wall-trims` tests still pass (mm-unit scenes unchanged); the bug was a latent footgun that only manifested in scenes with non-mm units.

**Out of scope (Phase 1G+).**

- ESC from `awaitingAlignment` currently deactivates the tool entirely (same as ESC from any other phase). A future incremental-back behaviour ("ESC at `awaitingAlignment` вЖТ back to `awaitingEnd` so the user can re-pick the end") is not part of Phase 1F. **вЖТ Implemented in Phase 1H (2026-05-29).**
- A keyboard shortcut to commit centered on click 2 (skipping alignment) is intentionally NOT provided вАФ the user explicitly requested mandatory 3 clicks.
- Curved + polyline kinds keep their existing flows. Curved already has a 3rd click (Bezier control); polyline uses Enter to finish. Adding a 4th alignment click on top is deferred until there is a concrete request.

**Phase 1G вАФ Hot-grip click-click move for the 4 corner grips** *(вЬЕ IMPLEMENTED 2026-05-28)*

**Motivation.** All wall grips used press-drag-release (mousedown вЖТ drag вЖТ mouseup commit) via `useUnifiedGripInteraction` (`idle вЖТ hovering вЖТ warm вЖТ dragging`). For the 4 asymmetric corner grips (Phase 1C-bis: `wall-corner-{start,end}-{pos,neg}`) the user requested the AutoCAD **hot grip** pattern: 1st click activates "move mode" (NOT a drag), the cursor moves the corner live with a dashed rubber-band leader + live wall ghost, and a 2nd click commits. Press-drag-release is removed **only** for these 4 corners; every other wall grip (start/end/midpoint/thickness/rotation/curve/vertex) keeps drag.

**FSM extension.** `UnifiedGripPhase` gains `'hotGrip'` (distinct from `dragging` so the press-drag-release mouseup-commit logic does NOT fire for corners). Two refs drive it: `hotGripAwaitingFirstReleaseRef` (1st-click release vs later) and `hotGripMovedRef` (has the cursor left the anchor since arming):

```
mousedown on corner grip (phaseвЙ†hotGrip) вЖТ enter hotGrip (activeGrip, anchor=grip.pos, awaiting=true, moved=false)
mouseup  (awaiting)                        вЖТ arm: clear awaiting, re-baseline moved=false, stay hot (NO commit/deselect)
mousemove (hotGrip, moved>ќµ from anchor)   вЖТ setCurrentWorldPos + moved=true вЖТ live ghost + rubber band
mousedown (phase=hotGrip, 2nd click)       вЖТ consume (suppress lasso/selection); commit fires on its mouseup
mouseup  (!awaiting & moved)               вЖТ commit (delta = upWorldPos вИТ anchor) вЖТ resetToIdle
mouseup  (!awaiting & !moved)              вЖТ stay: redundant same-spot release вЖТ stay hot (NO reset)
ESC / right-click (hotGrip)                вЖТ resetToIdle (cancel, no commit)
selection change                           вЖТ reset refs (existing effect)
```

**Why the `stay` guard (the reset-on-release bug).** `handleMouseUp` is `async` with NO `await` before the hot-grip branch, so its `finally` (mutex release) runs **synchronously**. The canvas + container `onMouseUp` pair therefore both pass the mutex within one tick: without a guard the 2nd fire saw `awaiting=false` вЖТ `commit` вЖТ a zero-delta no-op commit that STILL ran `resetToIdle`, dropping back to `idle` on the 1st click. Symptom: the rubber-band only appeared while the button was held. Fix: a `commit` requires `moved=true`; a stray same-spot release (no intervening mousemove) resolves to `stay` and keeps the wall hot. This also makes press-drag-release on a corner resolve to `arm` (not commit), enforcing the click-click contract Giorgio asked for even when the user instinctively drags.

**Forgiving entry.** On mousedown, if `findNearestGrip` just misses the handle but a wall corner grip is currently highlighted (`hoveredGrip`), that hovered corner is taken as the hit вАФ "it's blue вЖТ the click grabs it", even with a slightly-off click.

**Why commit on the 2nd mouseup (not mousedown):** `mouse-handler-up.ts` already applies OSNAP to the up world point, so the commit point is snapped вАФ unlike the un-snapped grip mousedown path. The dispatcher `commitDxfGripDragModeAware` checks `grip.wallGripKind` first, so the corner always routes to `commitWallGripDrag` (parametric `moveCorner` + `UpdateWallParamsCommand`) regardless of GripMode. **No new transform/commit code** вАФ Phase 1C-bis math is reused as-is.

**onCanvasClick suppression.** The `handleGripMouseUp` projection returns `wasDragging` (now `|| phase==='hotGrip'`) which gates the upstream `onCanvasClick`, so neither the 1st-click release nor the commit deselects the wall. `isDraggingGrip`/`isFollowingGrip` also include `hotGrip` so the upstream snap applies to the live rubber-band move and the lasso gate stays closed on the 2nd click.

**ADR-040 compliance.** Hot-grip state lives in `useUnifiedGripInteraction` as React state, exactly mirroring the existing `dragging` re-render path (no NEW store, no orchestrator `useSyncExternalStore`). The dashed rubber-band is drawn in the existing micro-leaf `useGripGhostPreview` (mounted via `GripDragPreviewMount`), not in any orchestrator.

**Files.**

- [x] **NEW** `hooks/grips/wall-hot-grip-fsm.ts` вАФ pure (zero React) SSoT for the decisions: `WALL_CORNER_GRIP_KINDS`, `isWallCornerGripKind()`, `resolveHotGripMouseDown()` вЖТ `enter|consume|none`, `resolveHotGripMouseUp()` вЖТ `arm|set-base|stay|commit|none` (the `stay`/`set-base` actions land with 1G.2 below).
- [x] **NEW** `hooks/grips/__tests__/wall-hot-grip-fsm.test.ts` вАФ predicate (corner/move/rotate vs others + null) + every mousedown/mouseup transition across all phases/steps.
- [x] `hooks/grips/unified-grip-types.ts` вАФ `UnifiedGripPhase` += `'hotGrip'`.
- [x] `hooks/grip-computation.ts` вАФ `DxfGripDragPreview` += `hotGrip?: boolean`.
- [x] `hooks/grips/grip-projections.ts` вАФ `buildDxfDragPreview` guard accepts `hotGrip`, emits the `hotGrip` flag.
- [x] `hooks/grips/useUnifiedGripInteraction.ts` вАФ `hotGripAwaitingFirstReleaseRef` + `hotGripMovedRef`; `handleMouseDown` enter (with forgiving hovered-corner fallback) / consume; `handleMouseMove` full-rate follow + sets `moved` once the cursor leaves the anchor; `handleMouseUp` arm / stay / commit branch; `handleEscape` += hotGrip; `resetToIdle` + selection-change effect reset both refs; `dxfProjection` `isDxfFollowing` + suppress + `wasDragging` extensions.
- [x] `hooks/grips/useGripContextMenuController.ts` вАФ right-click during `hotGrip` aborts the move (`handleEscape`) instead of opening the grip menu.
- [x] `hooks/tools/useGripGhostPreview.ts` вАФ `drawFrame` strokes a dashed (`[6,4]`) leader anchorвЖТcursor via `CoordinateTransforms.worldToScreen` when `dragPreview.hotGrip`, drawn before the ghost short-circuit so it shows even on a thickness clamp.

**Phase 1G.2 вАФ Move & Rotation glyphs (3-click with explicit base / centre pick)** *(вЬЕ IMPLEMENTED 2026-05-28)*

Extends the hot-grip flow to the **move glyph** (`wall-midpoint`, 4-arrow) and the **rotation glyph** (`wall-rotation`). Unlike corners (where the grip IS the anchor вЖТ 2 clicks), these use **3 clicks** so the user picks an explicit base point / rotation centre (Giorgio's choice, confirmed 2026-05-28):

```
MOVE:    click glyph вЖТ click = base point вЖТ move (rubber-band baseвЖТcursor, wall translates) вЖТ click = commit
ROTATE:  click glyph вЖТ click = rotation centre вЖТ move (rubber-band centreвЖТcursor, wall rotates around it) вЖТ click = commit
```

- **`hotGripOpRef`** вИИ `corner | move | rotate` + **`hotGripStepRef`** вИИ `await-base | tracking`. Corner enters straight into `tracking` (anchor = grip); move/rotate enter `await-base` (no anchor/preview until the centre/base is picked). The mouseup FSM gains `'set-base'` (the 2nd click that declares the base/centre, on mouseup so it is OSNAP-snapped).
- **MOVE** reuses the existing `wall-midpoint` translate: anchor = base, `delta = cursor вИТ base`, `moveMidpoint` translates the whole wall. The rubber-band is baseвЖТcursor (`anchorPos + delta`).
- **ROTATE** rotates around the picked centre, not the wall midpoint. `rotateWall` gains an optional **`pivot`** (`WallGripDragInput.pivot`); the swept angle stays anchor-relative against a **reference arm** (the cursor at the first move after the centre pick) so there is no snap. The pivot+anchor reach the commit via **`WallRotateHotGripStore`** (the same store-bridge pattern the commit adapters already use for `GripBasePointStore` / `ShiftKeyTracker`, because the generic dispatcher only forwards `(grip, delta)`). The rubber-band starts at the centre (`rotatePivot`) вЖТ cursor.
- Live ghost: `DxfGripDragPreview.rotatePivot` + `EntityPreviewTransform.rotatePivot` thread the centre to `applyWallGripDrag` so the preview rotates around it.
- **Double-fire fix (2026-05-28).** The same-tick canvas+container mouseup pair collapsed move/rotate into 2 clicks: on the 1st click, `fire1='arm'` then `fire2` (still `await-base`, no mousemove between) prematurely resolved `'set-base'` at the glyph position вАФ burning 2 steps in 1 click. Fix: `resolveHotGripMouseUp` now evaluates `!movedSinceArm вЖТ 'stay'` **before** the `await-base вЖТ 'set-base'` branch (order: `none вЖТ arm вЖТ stay вЖТ set-base вЖТ commit`), and `handleMouseMove` marks `hotGripMovedRef=true` on **any** real cursor move while `step==='await-base'`. A stray same-tick release produces no mousemove вЖТ stays `moved=false` вЖТ `'stay'`; only a deliberate 2nd click (preceded by movement) resolves `'set-base'`. Corners (2-click) are unaffected (they already require movement before commit).

**Files (Phase 1G.2): 1 NEW + 6 MOD.**
- [x] **NEW** `bim/walls/wall-rotate-hotgrip-store.ts` вАФ `{ pivot, anchor }` commit-bridge singleton.
- [x] `bim/walls/wall-grip-transforms.ts` вАФ `WallGripDragInput.pivot?`; `rotateWall` rotates around `pivot ?? midpoint`.
- [x] `hooks/grips/wall-hot-grip-fsm.ts` вАФ `hotGripOpForKind` / `isWallHotGripKind` / `initialHotGripStep`; `resolveHotGripMouseUp(phase, awaiting, step, moved)` += `'set-base'`.
- [x] `hooks/grip-computation.ts` + `rendering/ghost/apply-entity-preview.ts` вАФ `rotatePivot?` threaded to `applyWallGripDrag` ghost.
- [x] `hooks/tools/useGripGhostPreview.ts` вАФ rubber-band start = `rotatePivot ?? anchorPos`.
- [x] `hooks/grips/grip-parametric-commits.ts` вАФ `commitWallGripDrag` reads `WallRotateHotGripStore` for `wall-rotation` (pivot + reference anchor).
- [x] `hooks/grips/useUnifiedGripInteraction.ts` вАФ `hotGripOpRef` / `hotGripStepRef` / `hotGripBaseRef`; enter is op-aware; `set-base` step; rotate reference-arm capture on first move; `dxfDragPreview` surfaces `rotatePivot`.

**SRP split (file-size compliance, SOS N.7.1).** Phase 1G pushed `useUnifiedGripInteraction.ts` past the 500-line limit. The two large mouse-event bodies were extracted **verbatim** into **NEW** `hooks/grips/grip-mouse-handlers.ts` (`runGripMouseDown` / `runGripMouseUp`, driven by a destructured context object) вАФ pure relocation, zero behaviour change. Hook drops to ~394 lines; the new module is ~406. The hook's `useCallback` wrappers just forward to the two functions with the same dependency arrays.

**Out of scope.** No change to non-hot-grip wall grips (start/end/thickness/curve/vertex stay drag). Hot-grip is NOT added to stair/beam/slab/column grips. The corner `moveCorner` math is untouched.

**Phase 1G.3 вАФ Rotation glyph = AutoCAD "ROTATE вЖТ Reference" (6 clicks)** *(вЬЕ IMPLEMENTED 2026-05-28)*

Giorgio's choice (confirmed 2026-05-28): the rotation glyph **always** runs the reference flow вАФ the simple free-drag rotate is removed. Six clicks total; the wall spins so the **reference direction maps onto the alignment direction**:

```
1 click glyph вЖТ 2 click rotation centre вЖТ 3+4 click reference line (existing direction)
              вЖТ 5+6 click alignment line (target direction) вЖТ commit
```

- **Steps.** `HotGripStep` gains `await-ref-start | await-ref-end | await-align-start | await-align-end`. `advanceHotGripStep(op, step)` is the pure progression table (terminal вЗФ next step equals current); `resolveHotGripMouseUp(op, вА¶)` now takes the op and returns `'advance'` (non-terminal pick) or `'commit'` (terminal). Move stays 3-click (`await-base вЖТ tracking`), corner stays 2-click (`tracking`). Each deliberate (moved) click advances; a same-tick stray release (no mousemove) вЖТ `'stay'` (the 1G.2 double-fire guard, generalised to every step).
- **Angle without touching the transform.** No change to `rotateWall` / `WallGripDragInput`. The reference direction is injected through the existing `pivot`+`anchor` bridge: on the reference-line completion the anchor is set to `pivot + refDir`, and the commit passes `delta = alignDir вИТ refDir`. Then `currentPos = anchor + delta = pivot + alignDir`, so `rotateWall` sweeps `atan2(alignDir) вИТ atan2(refDir)` around the centre вАФ exactly the reference rotation. `WallRotateHotGripStore` carries `{pivot, anchor}` to the commit as before.
- **Live preview.** `buildRotateReferencePreview` (in `grip-projections.ts`) drives the per-step ghost: dashed `rotateRefLine` (traced reference) + `rotateAlignLine` (live alignment) on the preview canvas, plus the rotating wall ghost during `await-align-end` (reusing the delta+pivot ghost pipeline via the same `anchor = pivot + refDir` identity). New display-only fields `DxfGripDragPreview.rotateRefLine` / `.rotateAlignLine`; `useGripGhostPreview` draws them (and suppresses the single-leader rubber-band when they are present).
- **Hints.** Per-step toolbar prompts (`pickRotateCentre` / `pickRefLineStart` / `pickRefLineEnd` / `pickAlignStart` / `pickAlignEnd`, + `pickMoveBase` for move) via `toolHintOverrideStore`; cleared on reset.

**Files (Phase 1G.3): 1 NEW + 7 MOD.** NEW `grip-hotgrip-actions.ts` (`advanceHotGripPick` + `commitRotateReference` + step hints вАФ extracted to keep `grip-mouse-handlers.ts` under the 500-line limit, SOS N.7.1). MOD: `wall-hot-grip-fsm.ts` (steps + `advanceHotGripStep` + `resolveHotGripMouseUp` op signature), `grip-mouse-handlers.ts` (dispatch `advance`/`commit` + enter hint), `useUnifiedGripInteraction.ts` (ref/align refs + preview routing + reset), `grip-computation.ts` (preview guide-line fields), `grip-projections.ts` (`buildRotateReferencePreview`), `useGripGhostPreview.ts` (dashed segments), `el`/`en` `tool-hints.json` (5 step prompts). `wall-grip-transforms.ts` UNCHANGED (angle injected via the existing `pivot`+`anchor` bridge). Tests: `wall-hot-grip-fsm.test.ts` (54/54 incl. `advanceHotGripStep` + rotate chain).

**Phase 1G.4 вАФ Ctrl at the terminal MOVE click = COPY (AutoCAD MOVEвЖТCOPY)** *(вЬЕ IMPLEMENTED 2026-05-29)*

Giorgio's choice (confirmed 2026-05-29): on the wall **move** glyph (`wall-midpoint`, 3-click flow), holding **Ctrl** (or **вМШ** on macOS) at the terminal (destination) click **copies** the wall to that point instead of translating it вАФ exactly AutoCAD's `MOVE` вЖТ `COPY` modifier. **Single copy**: the original is left in place, one copy is produced, and the hot-grip flow resets (no continuous copy chain).

- **Modifier read.** The destination mouseup loses its native event (`mouse-handler-up` вЖТ `handleMouseUp(worldPos)`), so a new vanilla singleton `keyboard/CtrlKeyTracker.ts` (direct sibling of `ShiftKeyTracker`, tracks `Control`+`Meta`) supplies the live state at commit time. Read in `grip-mouse-handlers.runGripMouseUp` only on the terminal click of a `'move'` hot-grip whose grip is `wall-midpoint`.
- **Copy = re-create, not transform.** Instead of a command, the copy mirrors how new walls are born: `commitWallCopy` (`grip-parametric-commits.ts`) computes the translated params via the SAME `applyWallGripDrag('wall-midpoint', вА¶)` whole-wall translate the move uses, then `buildWallEntity(translated, wall.layerId, wall.kind, sceneUnits)` mints a fresh enterprise wall ID (N.6) + recomputed geometry, and inserts it through the shared `addWallToScene` SSoT.
- **`addWallToScene` SSoT (new).** The body of `useSpecialTools.onWallCreated` (append вЖТ `computeWallTrims`/`applyTrimPatches` вЖТ `setLevelScene` вЖТ emit `drawing:entity-created` with tool `'wall'`) is extracted to `bim/walls/add-wall-to-scene.ts` and now serves BOTH the draw tool and the copy path (N.0.2 вАФ no copy-paste of the persistence trigger). The broadcast is what `useWallPersistence` waits on to schedule the first Firestore save, so the copy persists like a drawn wall.
- **Hint.** During the live move (`step === 'tracking'`) the toolbar shows `tool-hints:gripContextMenu.prompts.moveOrCopy` (¬ЂќЪќїќєќЇ ќ≥ќєќ± ѕДќњѕАќњќЄќ≠ѕДќЈѕГќЈ ¬Ј Ctrl = ќ±ќљѕДќєќ≥ѕБќ±ѕЖќЃ¬ї).

**Files (Phase 1G.4): 2 NEW + 4 MOD + 1 NEW test.** NEW `keyboard/CtrlKeyTracker.ts`, `bim/walls/add-wall-to-scene.ts`. MOD: `hooks/tools/useSpecialTools.ts` (`onWallCreated` вЖТ `addWallToScene` SSoT), `hooks/grips/grip-parametric-commits.ts` (`commitWallCopy`), `hooks/grips/grip-mouse-handlers.ts` (Ctrl branch at move commit), `hooks/grips/grip-hotgrip-actions.ts` + `el`/`en` `tool-hints.json` (`moveOrCopy` hint). Test: `bim/walls/__tests__/add-wall-to-scene.test.ts` (7 cases вАФ SSoT insert + copy translate/fresh-ID/original-untouched + no-op guards). `wall-grip-transforms.ts` UNCHANGED (copy reuses the move translate). 60/60 wall-grip + hot-grip + new tests PASS.

**Phase 7.2 fix вАФ command-path copy clones now persist (`bim-clone-persistence` SSoT)** *(вЬЕ IMPLEMENTED 2026-06-01)*

**Bug (Giorgio live test 2026-06-01, HANDOFFS/2026-06-01_BIM_copy-mirror-persistence-bug).** Copy+mirror ќµќљѕМѕВ BIM ѕГѕДќњќєѕЗќµќѓќњѕЕ (mirror dialog ¬ЂќЇѕБќђѕДќ± ќ±ѕБѕЗќєќЇѕМ;¬ї вЖТ ќЭќСќЩ, `keepOriginals=true`) ќµќЉѕЖќђќљќєќґќµ ѕДќњ ќ±ќљѕДќѓќ≥ѕБќ±ѕЖќњ ќЇќ±ќє ќ±ѕЕѕДѕМ **ќ±ѕГѕДѕБќ±ѕАќєќ±ќѓќ± ќµќЊќ±ѕЖќ±ќљќєќґѕМѕДќ±ќљ**. Root cause: `MirrorEntityCommand.execute()` (copy branch) вАФ ќЇќ±ќє ќњќЉќњќѓѕЙѕВ `BimCopyCommand.execute()` (BIM Copy tool) вАФ ќ≠ќЇќ±ќљќ±ќљ ѕГќЇќ≠ѕДќњ `sceneManager.addEntity(clone)` ќЉќµ `generateEntityId()`, **ѕЗѕЙѕБќѓѕВ** ѕДќњ `drawing:entity-created` broadcast. ќ§ќњ Firestore subscription (`use*Persistence`) ќЄќµѕЙѕБќµќѓ ќЇќђќЄќµ scene entity ѕАќњѕЕ ќіќµќљ ќ≠ѕЗќµќє doc/dirty/pending ќµќ≥ќ≥ѕБќ±ѕЖќЃ ѕЙѕВ `mutated` ќЇќ±ќє ѕДќњ ѕАќµѕДќђќµќє ѕГѕДќњ ќµѕАѕМќЉќµќљќњ snapshot. (In-place mirror `keepOriginals=false` ќФќХќЭ ќµѕАќЈѕБќµќ±ќґѕМѕДќ±ќљ вАФ ќЉќµѕДќ±ќїќїќђѕГѕГќµќє ќЃќіќЈ-persisted ѕГѕДќњќєѕЗќµќѓќњ ѕАќњѕЕ ѕДќњ `useBimEntityMovedPersistEffect` ќЊќ±ќљќ±ѕГѕОќґќµќє.)

- **SSoT (new).** `bim/transforms/bim-clone-persistence.ts` вАФ `mintBimCloneIdentity(type)` (per-type enterprise ID, N.6, + **fresh `ifcGuid`** ѕОѕГѕДќµ ќљќ± ќЉќЈќљ ѕГѕЕќ≥ќЇѕБќњѕНќµѕДќ±ќє ѕДќњ IFC GlobalId ќЉќµ ѕДќЈќљ ѕАќЈќ≥ќЃ) + `broadcastBimCloneCreated` (emit `drawing:entity-created`, tool = type вЖТ ѕАѕБѕОѕДќњ Firestore save) + `broadcastBimCloneDeleted` (emit per-type `bim:*-delete-requested` вЖТ Firestore delete + tombstone, ѕГѕДќњ undo) + `broadcastBimCloneRestored` (emit `bim:entity-restore-requested` source `'redo-restore'` вЖТ clear tombstone + re-save, ѕГѕДќњ redo). ќ£ѕЕќЉќЉќµѕДѕБќєќЇѕМ ќ±ќљѕДќѓѕГѕДѕБќњѕЖќњ ѕДќњѕЕ `DeleteEntityCommand` (create вЖФ delete, redo вЖФ restore).
- **`MirrorEntityCommand`.** Copy branch ѕЗѕДќѓќґќµќє clone ќЉќµ `mintBimCloneIdentity` (BIM) ќЃ `generateEntityId()` (non-BIM) + `broadcastBimCloneCreated`. ќСѕАќњќЄќЈќЇќµѕНќµќє ќЯќЫќЯќЪќЫќЧќ°ќС ѕДќ± clones (ѕМѕЗќє ќЉѕМќљќњ ids) вЖТ undo/redo **id-stable** (redo ќЊќ±ќљќ±-ѕАѕБќњѕГќЄќ≠ѕДќµќє ѕДќњ ќЩќФќЩќЯ entity ќ±ќљѕДќѓ ќљќ± ќЇѕМќ≤ќµќє ќљќ≠ќњ id ѕАќњѕЕ ќЄќ± ќњѕБѕЖќђќљќµѕЕќµ ѕДќњ ѕАѕБќњќЈќ≥ќњѕНќЉќµќљќњ Firestore doc) + emit delete/restore.

**Phase 1H вАФ ESC incremental-back from `awaitingAlignment`** *(вЬЕ IMPLEMENTED 2026-05-29)*

Closes the Phase 1F out-of-scope item. In the straight-wall 3-click flow (`awaitingStart вЖТ awaitingEnd вЖТ awaitingAlignment вЖТ commit`), pressing **ESC** while in `awaitingAlignment` (end picked, lateral side not yet picked) now **steps back one pick** to `awaitingEnd` вАФ the picked end is dropped, the start is kept, and the user can re-pick the end. Previously ESC deactivated the whole tool (generic DRAW_TOOL cancel). Revit "Modify | Place Wall" parity: Esc backs out one pick at a time rather than exiting the command.

- **Self-contained in the FSM owner.** `useWallTool` gains a pure `backToAwaitingEnd()` method (`awaitingAlignment вЖТ awaitingEnd`, clears `endPoint` + `error`, keeps `startPoint`; no-op + returns `false` outside `awaitingAlignment`). Curved/polyline kinds never reach `awaitingAlignment`, so this is straight-only by construction.
- **ESC bus wiring.** `useWallTool` registers a single `useEscapeHandler` (`id: 'wall-tool/alignment-back'`) at a **new priority `ESC_PRIORITY.WALL_ALIGNMENT_BACK` (P525)** вАФ slotted between `DRAW_TOOL` (500) and `DIM_TOOL` (550) so it consumes ESC **before** the generic "cancel drawing" handler in `useKeyboardShortcuts` deactivates the tool. `canHandle` gates on `phase === 'awaitingAlignment'`, so in every other phase the generic cancel keeps its existing behaviour (deactivate). No threading through `CanvasSection` params вАФ the handler lives with the FSM it mutates (SRP).
- **Single back-step only.** ESC from `awaitingEnd` (or any non-alignment phase) still routes to the generic DRAW_TOOL cancel вЖТ deactivates. So one ESC backs the side-pick out to the end-pick; a second ESC exits the tool вАФ matching the incremental Revit/AutoCAD escape ladder.

**Files (Phase 1H): 3 MOD.**
- [x] `systems/escape-bus/escape-priority.ts` вАФ new `WALL_ALIGNMENT_BACK: 525` constant + doc.
- [x] `hooks/drawing/useWallTool.ts` вАФ `backToAwaitingEnd()` method (exposed on `UseWallToolResult`) + `useEscapeHandler` registration at P525.
- [x] `hooks/drawing/__tests__/useWallTool.test.tsx` вАФ 4 new tests (step-back transition + re-pick end + no-op outside alignment + ESC-key routes through bus). 21/21 PASS. `EscapeCommandBus` 24/24 + `cross-mode-shortcuts` 22/22 still PASS.

**Phase 1J вАФ ¬Ђќ§ќњќѓѕЗќњѕВ ѕАќђќљѕЙ ѕГќµ ќњќљѕДѕМѕДќЈѕДќ± 2ќФ¬ї (Wall on existing 2D entity)** *(вЬЕ IMPLEMENTED 2026-05-30)*

**Motivation (Giorgio 2026-05-30).** ќСќљѕДќѓ ќµќїќµѕНќЄќµѕБќЈѕВ ѕГѕЗќµќіќѓќ±ѕГќЈѕВ click-by-click, ќњ ѕЗѕБќЃѕГѕДќЈѕВ ќіќµќѓѕЗќљќµќє ќЉќєќ± **ѕЕѕАќђѕБѕЗќњѕЕѕГќ± 2ќФ ќњќљѕДѕМѕДќЈѕДќ±** (ќ≥ѕБќ±ќЉќЉќЃ ќЃ ќњѕБќЄќњќ≥ѕОќљќєќњ/ќЇќїќµќєѕГѕДѕМ polyline) ќ±ѕАѕМ ѕДќњ underlay ќЇќ±ќє ќњ ѕДќњќѓѕЗќњѕВ ¬ЂќЇќњѕЕќЉѕАѕОќљќµќє¬ї ѕАќђќљѕЙ ѕДќЈѕВ. Industry parity: Revit "Pick Lines" + Location Line/flip, ArchiCAD "Magic Wand". ќЭќ≠ќ± ќµѕАќєќїќњќ≥ќЃ ѕГѕДќњ dropdown ¬ЂќФќњќЉќєќЇќђ ќ£ѕДќњќєѕЗќµќѓќ±¬ї вЖТ ¬Ђќ§ќњќѓѕЗќњѕВ ѕАќђќљѕЙ ѕГќµ ќњќљѕДѕМѕДќЈѕДќ± 2ќФ¬ї.

**ќ£ќЈќЉќ±ѕГќєќњќїќњќ≥ќѓќ± (ќµќљќєќ±ќѓќ±, 2 ќЇќїќєќЇ вАФ ѕГѕЕќЉќЉќµѕДѕБќєќЇќЃ ќ≥ќєќ± ќ≥ѕБќ±ќЉќЉќЃ & ќњѕБќЄќњќ≥ѕОќљќєќњ).**
- **ќЪќїќєќЇ 1 = ќіќєќђќїќµќЊќµ ќњќљѕДѕМѕДќЈѕДќ±** (hit-test). **ќЪќїќєќЇ 2 = ѕАќїќµѕЕѕБќђ.**
- **ќУѕБќ±ќЉќЉќЃ** вЖТ ќ≠ќљќ±ѕВ ѕДќњќѓѕЗќњѕВ, ќѓќіќєќњ ќЉќЃќЇќњѕВ¬Ј ќЈ ѕАќ±ѕБќµќєќђ ќЉќ±ќЇѕБќєќђ ќ±ѕАѕМ ѕДќњ side point ќЇќђќЄќµѕДќ±ќє ѕГѕДќЈ ќ≥ѕБќ±ќЉќЉќЃ, ќњ ѕДќњќѓѕЗќњѕВ ѕЖќњѕЕѕГќЇѕОќљќµќє ѕАѕБќњѕВ ѕДќњ side point (ќѓќіќєќ± semantics ќЉќµ ѕДќњ Phase 1F alignment offset).
- **ќЯѕБќЄќњќ≥ѕОќљќєќњ / ќЇќїќµќєѕГѕДѕМ polyline** вЖТ ќ≠ќљќ±ѕВ ѕДќњќѓѕЗќњѕВ ќ±ќљќђ ќ±ќЇќЉќЃ. Side point **ќЬќХќ£ќС** вЖТ ќµѕГѕЙѕДќµѕБќєќЇќњќѓ ѕДќњќѓѕЗќњќє (ќµќЊѕЙѕДќµѕБќєќЇќЃ ѕАќ±ѕБќµќєќђ ѕГѕДќњ ѕАќµѕБќѓќ≥ѕБќ±ќЉќЉќ±)¬Ј **ќХќЮќ©** вЖТ ќµќЊѕЙѕДќµѕБќєќЇќњќѓ (ќµѕГѕЙѕДќµѕБќєќЇќЃ ѕАќ±ѕБќµќєќђ ѕГѕДќњ ѕАќµѕБќѓќ≥ѕБќ±ќЉќЉќ±). ќУѕЙќљќєќ±ќЇќ≠ѕВ ќµќљѕОѕГќµќєѕВ (miter/bevel) ѕАѕБќњќЇѕНѕАѕДќњѕЕќљ ќ±ѕЕѕДѕМќЉќ±ѕДќ± ќ≥ќєќ±ѕДќѓ ќЇќђќЄќµ ѕДќњќѓѕЗќњѕВ ѕАќµѕБќљќђ ќ±ѕАѕМ ѕДќњ `addWallToScene` вЖТ `computeWallTrims` ѕГќµ ѕМќїќњѕЕѕВ ѕДќњѕЕѕВ ѕДќњќѓѕЗќњѕЕѕВ.

**ќЬќ≠ќ≥ќєѕГѕДќњ reuse вАФ ќЉќЈќіќ≠ќљ ќіќєѕАќїќЃ geometry math.** ќЧ ќљќ≠ќ± ќіќњѕЕќїќµќєќђ ќµќѓќљќ±ќє **ќ≥ќ≠ѕЖѕЕѕБќ±**: ѕДќњ hit-test (`testEntityHit`/`pointToLineDistance` SSoT), ѕДќњ ќЉќ≠ѕГќ±/ќ≠ќЊѕЙ (`isPointInPolygon`), ќЇќ±ќє ќњќє wall builders (`buildDefaultWallParams` ќЉќµ alignmentPoint + `buildWallEntity`) ѕАѕБќњѕЛѕАќЃѕБѕЗќ±ќљ. ќ§ќњ ѕАќєќњ ќіѕНѕГќЇќњќїќњ ќЇќњќЉќЉќђѕДќє (axis offset ѕОѕГѕДќµ ќЈ ѕАќ±ѕБќµќєќђ ќљќ± ќЇќђќЄќµѕДќ±ќє ѕГѕДќЈ ќ≥ѕБќ±ќЉќЉќЃ) ќµќѓќљќ±ќє ѕДќњ ќѓќіќєќњ `computeWallAlignmentOffset` ѕДќњѕЕ Phase 1F.

**Design вАФ ќ≠ќљќ± tool, ќіѕНќњ placement modes.** ќЭќ≠ќњ `ToolType 'wall-on-entity'` (ѕДќњ ribbon variant click ќЇќђќљќµќє `onToolChange(commandKey)`). ќ§ќњ ќЩќФќЩќЯ `useWallTool` ќµќЊѕЕѕАќЈѕБќµѕДќµќѓ `'wall'` (freehand) ќЇќ±ќє `'wall-on-entity'` ќЉќ≠ѕГѕЙ ќµѕГѕЙѕДќµѕБќєќЇќњѕН `placementMode: 'freehand' | 'on-entity'` вАФ ќЉќЈќіќ≠ќљ ќіќєѕАќїѕМ tool. Click routing ѕАќµѕБќљќђ **raw** worldPoint (ѕМѕЗќє ORTHO/POLAR-constrained) ѕМѕДќ±ќљ on-entity, ќ≥ќєќ±ѕДќѓ ќіќµќѓѕЗќљќњѕЕќЉќµ ѕЕѕАќђѕБѕЗќњѕЕѕГќ± ќ≥ќµѕЙќЉќµѕДѕБќѓќ±.

**Out of scope / limitations.**
- RECTANGLE/closed polygons ќ±ќљѕДќєќЉќµѕДѕЙѕАќѓќґќњќљѕДќ±ќє axis-aligned ѕЙѕВ ѕАѕБќњѕВ ѕДќєѕВ ќЇќњѕБѕЕѕЖќ≠ѕВ (ignore `rotation`)¬Ј side-test ќЉќµ vertex-centroid вЖТ ѕГѕЙѕГѕДѕМ ќ≥ќєќ± ќЇѕЕѕБѕДќђ ѕГѕЗќЃќЉќ±ѕДќ± (ќњѕБќЄќњќ≥ѕОќљќєќ±/ѕДѕЕѕАќєќЇќђ ќіѕЙќЉќђѕДќєќ±), ѕМѕЗќє ќµќ≥ќ≥ѕЕќЈќЉќ≠ќљќ± ќ≥ќєќ± non-convex.
- ќФќµќљ ѕЕѕАќђѕБѕЗќµќє rubber-band ghost ќ≥ќєќ± closed sources (ќЉѕМќљќњ ќ≥ќєќ± line). рЯФі browser verify ќµќЇќЇѕБќµќЉќµќѓ.

**Phase 1J runtime fixes (Giorgio live test 2026-05-30) вАФ 2 bugs + hover/grip affordance.**
- **Bug A вАФ ѕДќњ ќњѕБќЄќњќ≥ѕОќљќєќњ ќіќµќљ ќіќЈќЉќєќњѕЕѕБќ≥ќњѕНѕГќµ ѕДќњќѓѕЗќњѕЕѕВ.** Root cause: ќњ rectangle drawing builder (`drawing-entity-builders.ts`) ќ±ѕАќњќЄќЈќЇќµѕНќµќє **ќЉѕМќљќњ** `corner1`/`corner2` ќЇќ±ќє ќ±ѕЖќЃќљќµќє `x/y/width/height` **undefined**. ќ§ќњ `rectangleCorners` ќіќєќђќ≤ќ±ќґќµ `e.x/e.width` вЖТ NaN corners вЖТ `polygonMinEdgeDistance` NaN вЖТ ѕАќњѕДќ≠ picked вЖТ ќЉќЈќіќ≠ќљ ѕДќњќѓѕЗќњќє. (ќЧ ќ≥ѕБќ±ќЉќЉќЃ ќіќњѕНќїќµѕЕќµ ќ≥ќєќ±ѕДќѓ `LineEntity` ќ≠ѕЗќµќє `start`/`end`.) Fix: `rectangleCorners` ѕАќїќ≠ќњќљ ѕАѕБќњѕДќєќЉќђ `x/y/width/height` ќ±ќїќїќђ ќЇќђќљќµќє **fallback ѕГќµ `corner1`/`corner2`** ќЉќµ normalize (Math.min/abs вЖТ ѕГѕЙѕГѕДѕМ ќЇќ±ќє ќ≥ќєќ± right-to-left / bottom-to-top draws). +2 regression tests.
- **Bug B вАФ ќіќµќљ ѕЖѕЙѕДќѓќґќњќљѕДќ±ќљ/ќµѕАќєќїќ≠ќ≥ќњќљѕДќ±ќљ ќњќє ќњќљѕДѕМѕДќЈѕДќµѕВ.** ќ§ќњ hover hit-test (`mouse-handler-move.ts`) ѕДѕБќ≠ѕЗќµќє ќЉѕМќљќњ ѕМѕДќ±ќљ `activeTool === 'select' || entityPickingActive`¬Ј ѕДќ± grips ќґѕЙќ≥ѕБќ±ѕЖќѓќґќњќљѕДќ±ќє ќЉѕМќљќњ ѕМѕДќ±ќљ `gripsAllowed` (`dxf-canvas-renderer.ts`: select/layering). Fix: (1) `CanvasSection.tsx` `entityPickingActive` ѕАќµѕБќєќїќ±ќЉќ≤ќђќљќµќє `wall-on-entity` вЖТ hover highlight¬Ј (2) `dxf-canvas-renderer.ts` `gripsAllowed` ѕАќµѕБќєќїќ±ќЉќ≤ќђќљќµќє `wall-on-entity` вЖТ grips ѕГѕДќЈќљ ќµѕАќєќїќµќ≥ќЉќ≠ќљќЈ ѕАќЈќ≥ќЃ¬Ј (3) `useCanvasClickHandler.ts` ѕГѕДќњ pick (click 1) ќЇќђќљќµќє `replaceEntitySelection([hoveredId])` (highlight + grips), ѕГѕДќњ place (click 2) `replaceEntitySelection([])` (clear).
- **ADR-040 touch:** `CanvasSection.tsx` + `canvas-v2/dxf-canvas/dxf-canvas-renderer.ts` ќµќѓќљќ±ќє micro-leaf/bitmap-cache ќ±ѕБѕЗќµќѓќ± вАФ ќ≤ќї. ADR-040 changelog (ќЉќѓќ± ќ≥ѕБќ±ќЉќЉќЃ, ќЉќЈќіќ≠ќљ ќ±ќїќїќ±ќ≥ќЃ ѕГѕДќњ subscription pattern¬Ј ќЉѕМќљќњ ќ≠ќљќ± tool-id ѕГќµ ѕЕѕАќђѕБѕЗќњќљѕДќ± boolean/`activeToolRef` ќ≠ќїќµќ≥ѕЗќњ).
- Files (runtime fixes): 5 MOD (`wall-from-entity.ts`, `CanvasSection.tsx`, `dxf-canvas-renderer.ts`, `useCanvasClickHandler.ts`, +2 tests ѕГѕДќњ `wall-from-entity.test.ts`). 39/39 PASS, tsc clean.

**Phase 1J geometry fix #2 вАФ ќњѕБќЄќњќ≥ѕОќљќєќњ ќ≥ѕЙќљќѓќµѕВ ќіќµќљ ќ≠ќЇќїќµќєќљќ±ќљ (Giorgio screenshot 2026-05-30).** ќ£ѕДќњ exterior ќњѕБќЄќњќ≥ѕОќљќєќњ ќЈ ќЇќђѕДѕЙ ѕАќїќµѕЕѕБќђ ќђѕЖќЈќљќµ ќЇќµќљќђ/ѕЕѕАќµѕБќ≤ќђѕГќµќєѕВ ѕГѕДќєѕВ 2 ќЇќђѕДѕЙ ќ≥ѕЙќљќѓќµѕВ. Root cause: ѕДќњ `buildWallsForClosed` ќ≠ѕЗѕДќєќґќµ ќЇќђќЄќµ ѕДќњќѓѕЗќњ ќЉќµ per-edge alignment offset (`computeWallAlignmentOffset` ќЉќµѕДќ±ѕДќњѕАќѓќґќµќє ќЪќСќЩ ѕДќ± ќіѕНќњ ќђќЇѕБќ± ќЇќ±ѕДќђ ѕДќњ ќѓќіќєќњ ќЇќђќЄќµѕДќњ ќіќєќђќљѕЕѕГќЉќ± ќ§ќЧќ£ ќЪќСќШќХ ќ±ќЇќЉќЃѕВ)¬Ј ќ≠ѕДѕГќє ќњќє ќђќЊќњќљќµѕВ ќіќєќ±ќіќњѕЗќєќЇѕОќљ ѕДќњќѓѕЗѕЙќљ **ќіќµќљ ѕГѕЕќљќ±ќљѕДќєѕМќљѕДќ±ќљ** ѕГѕДќєѕВ ќ≥ѕЙќљќѓќµѕВ (ѕДќњ ќЇќђќЄќµ ќђќЇѕБќњ ќЉќµѕДќ±ѕДќњѕАќєќґѕМѕДќ±ќљ ѕГќµ ќіќєќ±ѕЖќњѕБќµѕДќєќЇќЃ ќЇќђќЄќµѕДќЈ ѕЖќњѕБќђ) вАФ ѕДќњ `computeWallTrims` ѕДќњѕЕѕВ ќ≠ќљѕЙќљќµ ќЉѕМќљќњ ѕМѕГќњ ќЈ ќ±ѕАѕМѕГѕДќ±ѕГќЈ ќЃѕДќ±ќљ < `JOIN_THRESHOLD_MM` (200mm), ќњѕАѕМѕДќµ ѕГќµ ѕЗќњќљѕДѕБќњѕНѕВ ѕДќњќѓѕЗќњѕЕѕВ ќЈ ќ≥ѕЙќљќѓќ± ¬Ђќђќљќњќєќ≥ќµ¬ї. **Fix: exact miter offset** вАФ ќЇќђќЄќµ ќ±ќЇќЉќЃ ќЉќµѕДќ±ѕДќњѕАќѓќґќµѕДќ±ќє ѕАќ±ѕБќђќїќїќЈќїќ± ќЇќ±ѕДќђ halfThickness (centroid-ward normal, signed: inside +, outside вИТ) ќЇќ±ќє ќњќє **ќСќЮќЯќЭќХќ£ ќµќѓќљќ±ќє ќњќє ѕДќњќЉќ≠ѕВ ќіќєќ±ќіќњѕЗќєќЇѕОќљ offset edge-lines** (`intersectLines`). ќФќєќ±ќіќњѕЗќєќЇќњќѓ ѕДќњќѓѕЗќњќє ќЉќњќєѕБќђќґќњќљѕДќ±ќє **ќСќЪќ°ќЩќТќ©ќ£** ѕДќЈќљ ќѓќіќєќ± ќЇќњѕБѕЕѕЖќЃ вЖТ ќЇќ±ќЄќ±ѕБѕМ miter ѕГќµ ќЇќђќЄќµ ќ≥ѕЙќљќѓќ±/ѕАќђѕЗќњѕВ. ќФќµќљ ѕЗѕБќЈѕГќєќЉќњѕАќњќєќЃќЄќЈќЇќµ ѕДќњ `offsetPolyline`/`insetClosedPolygon` SSoT ќ≥ќєќ±ѕДќѓ ќµќѓќљќ±ќє averaged-normal approximation (under-offset ~50% ѕГќµ ќњѕБќЄќЃ ќ≥ѕЙќљќѓќ± вАФ ќЯќЪ ќ≥ќєќ± ќїќµѕАѕДќЃ ќЉѕМќљѕЙѕГќЈ, ќїќђќЄќњѕВ ќ≥ќєќ± ќ±ќЇѕБќєќ≤ќЃ ѕДќњѕАќњќЄќ≠ѕДќЈѕГќЈ ѕДќњќѓѕЗќњѕЕ). +SSoT `resolveWallThicknessMm` ѕГѕДќњ `wall-completion.ts` (reuse ѕГѕДќњ build + ѕГѕДќњ offset). +1 regression test (consecutive walls share endpoints exactly). 14/14 wall-from-entity PASS.

**Phase 1J 3D fix #3 вАФ ѕДќњќѓѕЗќњѕВ ќЉќµ ќЇќњѕНѕЖѕЙќЉќ± ќ≥ќєќљѕМѕДќ±ќљ ќњѕБќЄќњќ≥ѕОќљќєќњѕВ (ѕЗѕЙѕБќѓѕВ miter) ѕГѕДќњ 3D (Giorgio 3D report 2026-05-30).** ќ£ѕДќЈќљ ќЇќђѕДќњѕИќЈ ќњ ѕДќњќѓѕЗќњѕВ-ќЉќµ-ќЇќњѕНѕЖѕЙќЉќ± ќ≠ќіќµќєѕЗќљќµ ѕГѕЙѕГѕДќђ miter, ќ±ќїќїќђ ѕГѕДќњ 3D ќњќє ќђќЇѕБќµѕВ ѕДќњѕЕ ќ≥ќѓќљќњќљѕДќ±ќљ ѕДќµѕДѕБќђќ≥ѕЙќљќµѕВ ќЇќ±ќє ќіќµќљ ќ≠ќљѕЙќљќ±ќљ ќЉќµ ѕДќњѕЕѕВ ќ≥ќµќєѕДќњќљќєќЇќњѕНѕВ. Root cause (pre-existing, ќ±ќљќµќЊќђѕБѕДќЈѕДќњ ѕДќњѕЕ 2D feature вАФ ќ±ѕЖќњѕБќђ **ќЇќђќЄќµ** mitered ѕДќњќѓѕЗќњ ќЉќµ ќЇќњѕНѕЖѕЙќЉќ±): ќњ 3D converter ќ≠ѕЗќµќє 2 paths вАФ ѕЗѕЙѕБќѓѕВ ќЇќњѕНѕЖѕЙќЉќ± `buildWallShape(wall.geometry.outerEdge, innerEdge)` (mitered footprint, ѕГѕЙѕГѕДѕМ)¬Ј **ќЉќµ ќЇќњѕНѕЖѕЙќЉќ±** `buildWallMeshWithOpenings` (`wall-opening-extrude.ts`) ѕЗѕДќѓќґќµќє per-segment raw ќњѕБќЄќњќ≥ѕОќљќєќ± ќ±ѕАѕМ `getWallAxisVertices` (ќЉѕМќљќњ bevel, **ќ±ќ≥ќљќњќµќѓ `startMiter`/`endMiter`** ѕАќњѕЕ ќґќњѕЕќљ ќЉѕМќљќњ ѕГѕДќњ `wall.geometry.outerEdge/innerEdge`). **Fix: `buildStraightWallWithOpenings`** (ќљќ≠ќњ, ѕГѕДќњ `BimToThreeConverter.ts`) вАФ ќ≥ќєќ± straight ѕДќњќѓѕЗќњѕЕѕВ ѕГѕАќђќµќє ѕГќµ **ќЇќ±ѕДќ±ќЇѕМѕБѕЕѕЖќ± solid ќЇќњќЉќЉќђѕДќєќ±** (full-height jambs ќЉќµѕДќ±ќЊѕН/ќ≥ѕНѕБѕЙ ќ±ѕАѕМ ќЇќњѕЕѕЖѕОќЉќ±ѕДќ± + sill floorвЖТѕАќњќіќєќђ + header ѕАѕБќ≠ќЇќєвЖТѕДќ±ќ≤ќђќљќє), ќЇќђќЄќµ ќЇќњќЉќЉќђѕДќє = outer/inner **mitered** footprint quad (interpolated ќЇќ±ѕДќђ arc fraction) extruded ќЇќ±ѕДќ±ќЇѕМѕБѕЕѕЖќ± ќЉќ≠ѕГѕЙ ѕДѕЙќљ ќЇќњќєќљѕОќљ `buildShape`+`extrudeAndRotate` (ќѓќіќєќ± ѕГѕНќЉќ≤ќ±ѕГќЈ ќЉќµ ѕДќњ solid path). ќЯќє 2 ќђќЇѕБќµѕВ ѕЗѕБќЈѕГќєќЉќњѕАќњќєќњѕНќљ ѕДќ± ќСќЪќ°ќЩќТќЧ mitered corner points вЖТ ѕДќ± miter ќµѕАќєќ≤ќєѕОќљќњѕЕќљ. Curved/polyline ќЇѕБќ±ѕДќњѕНќљ ѕДќњ per-segment path (miters N/A ѕГќµ multi-segment ќђќЇѕБќµѕВ). 2 MOD (`BimToThreeConverter.ts`, +import `mmToSceneUnits`) + 4 tests (`wall-opening-extrude.test.ts`, incl. miter-corner regression). 10/10 PASS, tsc clean. рЯФі 3D browser verify ќµќЇќЇѕБќµќЉќµќѓ (ќіќµќљ ќµѕАќ±ќїќЈќЄќµѕНќµѕДќ±ќє mesh ќµќіѕО).

**Phase 1K вАФ ¬Ђќ§ќњќѓѕЗќњѕВ ѕГќµ ѕАќµѕБќєќњѕЗќЃ (4 ќ≥ѕБќ±ќЉќЉќ≠ѕВ)¬ї (Wall in region)** *(вЬЕ IMPLEMENTED 2026-05-30 вАФ modes A+B+C)*

**Motivation (Giorgio 2026-05-30).** ќЯ ѕЗѕБќЃѕГѕДќЈѕВ ќіќєќ±ќїќ≠ќ≥ќµќє **4 ќ±ќљќµќЊќђѕБѕДќЈѕДќµѕВ ќ≥ѕБќ±ќЉќЉќ≠ѕВ** ѕАќњѕЕ ќµќљѕОќљќњќљѕДќ±ќє ќЇќ±ќє ѕГѕЗќЈќЉќ±ѕДќѓќґќњѕЕќљ ќњѕБќЄќњќ≥ѕОќљќєќњ/ѕДќµѕДѕБќђќ≥ѕЙќљќњ, ќЇќ±ќє ќ±ѕАѕМ ѕДќњ dropdown ¬ЂќФќњќЉќєќЇќђ ќ£ѕДќњќєѕЗќµќѓќ±¬ї ќіќєќ±ќїќ≠ќ≥ќµќє ќљќ≠ќ± ќµќљѕДќњќїќЃ ¬Ђќ§ќњќѓѕЗќњѕВ ѕГќµ ѕАќµѕБќєќњѕЗќЃ (4 ќ≥ѕБќ±ќЉќЉќ≠ѕВ)¬ї: ќЉќ≠ѕГќ± ѕГѕДќЈќљ ѕАќµѕБќєќњѕЗќЃ ѕДќњѕАќњќЄќµѕДќµќѓѕДќ±ќє **ќХќЭќСќ£ ќ≥ќµќЉќђѕДќњѕВ ѕДќњќѓѕЗќњѕВ** BIM ќЉќµ **ќЉќЃќЇќњѕВ = ќЉќµќ≥ќђќїќЈ ѕАќїќµѕЕѕБќђ, ѕАќђѕЗќњѕВ = ќЉќєќЇѕБќЃ ѕАќїќµѕЕѕБќђ** (ќ≥ќµќЉќѓќґќµќє ѕДќњ ќњѕБќЄќњќ≥ѕОќљќєќњ). Command-first ѕБќњќЃ (CAD prototype: ѕАѕБѕОѕДќ± ќЈ ќµќљѕДќњќїќЃ, ќЉќµѕДќђ ѕДќ± ќ±ќљѕДќєќЇќµќѓќЉќµќљќ± вАФ ќµѕАќєќ≤ќµќ≤ќ±ќѓѕЙѕГќЈ Giorgio).

**ќ£ќЈќЉќ±ѕГќєќњќїќњќ≥ќѓќ± (command-first, ѕЕќ≤ѕБќєќіќєќЇќЃ ќµѕАќєќїќњќ≥ќЃ).**
- **Mode A вАФ 4 ќЇќїќєќЇ ќЉќѓќ±-ќЉќѓќ±:** ќЇќїќєќЇ ѕГќµ ќЇќђќЄќµ ќ≥ѕБќ±ќЉќЉќЃ¬Ј ќЉѕМќїќєѕВ 4 picks ќЇќїќµќѓќљќњѕЕќљ ќњѕБќЄќњќ≥ѕОќљќєќњ вЖТ ѕДќњѕАќњќЄќ≠ѕДќЈѕГќЈ. ќ£ѕЕќљќµѕЗѕМќЉќµќљќЈ ќїќµќєѕДќњѕЕѕБќ≥ќѓќ± (ќµѕАѕМќЉќµќљќњ ќњѕБќЄќњќ≥ѕОќљќєќњ)¬Ј ESC ќЇќ±ќЄќ±ѕБќѓќґќµќє ѕДќ± picks (ѕМѕЗќє deactivate).
- **Mode B вАФ 1 ќЇќїќєќЇ ќЉќ≠ѕГќ± ѕГѕДќЈќљ ѕАќµѕБќєќњѕЗќЃ:** ќЇќїќєќЇ ѕГќµ ќЇќµќљѕМ вЖТ ќµѕНѕБќµѕГќЈ ѕДќњѕЕ **ќµќїќђѕЗќєѕГѕДќњѕЕ** ќњѕБќЄќњќ≥ѕЙќљќѓќњѕЕ (ќ±ѕАѕМ ѕМќїќµѕВ ѕДќєѕВ scene ќ≥ѕБќ±ќЉќЉќ≠ѕВ) ѕАќњѕЕ ѕАќµѕБќєќЇќїќµќѓќµќє ѕДќњ ѕГќЈќЉќµќѓќњ вЖТ ѕДќњѕАќњќЄќ≠ѕДќЈѕГќЈ.
- **Mode C вАФ box-select:** вЬЕ **DONE (2026-05-30)** вАФ ќЉќ≠ѕГќ± ѕГѕДќЈќљ ќµќљѕДќњќїќЃ, ѕАќђѕДќ±-ѕГѕНѕБќµ-ќђѕГќµ вЖТ ќњѕБќЄќњќ≥ѕОќљќєќњ **window** (ќ±ѕБќєѕГѕДќµѕБќђвЖТќіќµќЊќєќђ) / **crossing** (ќіќµќЊќєќђвЖТќ±ѕБќєѕГѕДќµѕБќђ) ѕАќњѕЕ ќЉќ±ќґќµѕНќµќє ќ≥ѕБќ±ќЉќЉќ≠ѕВ¬Ј ѕГѕДќњ release ќ±ќљќєѕЗќљќµѕНќњќљѕДќ±ќє **ќЯќЫќС** ѕДќ± ќµѕГѕОќЇќїќµќєѕГѕДќ± ќњѕБќЄќњќ≥ѕОќљќєќ± вЖТ ѕЗѕДќѓќґќµѕДќ±ќє ќ≠ќљќ±ѕВ ќ≥ќµќЉќђѕДќњѕВ ѕДќњќѓѕЗќњѕВ ќ±ќљќђ ќњѕБќЄќњќ≥ѕОќљќєќњ. ќСѕАќїѕМ ќЇќїќєќЇ (ѕЗѕЙѕБќѓѕВ ѕГѕНѕБѕГќєќЉќњ) ѕАќ≠ѕЖѕДќµќє ѕГѕДќњ pick pipeline ѕДќњѕЕ mode A/B (ќ±ќЉќњќєќ≤ќ±ќѓќ± ќ±ѕАќњќЇќїќµќєѕМќЉќµќљќ± ќЉќ≠ѕГѕЙ `cursor.isSelecting`). Lasso ќЯќІќЩ (ѕГѕДќњ ќѓќіќєќњ ѕГѕНѕБѕГќєќЉќњ ќЉѕМќљќњ rectangle). Decoupled ќЉќ≠ѕГѕЙ `EventBus('bim:wall-region-box-select')` вАФ ќњ mouse-up handler ќЇќђќљќµќє `performSelection` (window/crossing) ќЇќ±ќє emit ќЉѕМќљќњ ѕДќ± `entityIds`¬Ј **ќіќµќљ ќ±ќ≥ќ≥ќѓќґќµќє ѕДќЈќљ ќµѕАќєќїќњќ≥ќЃ** (ќѓќіќєќњ ќЉќњѕДќѓќ≤ќњ ќЉќµ `crop:marquee-rect`). ќ§ќњ `useWallTool` ѕЖќєќїѕДѕБќђѕБќµќє ѕДќњ live scene ќЉќµ ѕДќ± ids вЖТ `extractLineSegments` вЖТ `findRectanglesFromSegments` вЖТ `commitInRegionRects(rects)`.

**ќ†ѕЕѕБќЃќљќ±ѕВ SSoT (corner-graph, ѕГѕДѕБќ±ќЉќЉќ≠ќљќ± ќњѕБќЄќњќ≥ѕОќљќєќ± OK).** ќЭќ≠ќњ `bim/walls/wall-in-region.ts`:
- `findRectanglesFromSegments(segments, tol)` вАФ ќЉќµѕБѕДќґќђѕБќµќє ќЇќњќљѕДќєќљќђ ќђќЇѕБќ± ѕГќµ ќЇѕМќЉќ≤ќњѕЕѕВ, ќ≤ѕБќѓѕГќЇќµќє 4-ќЇѕНќЇќїќњѕЕѕВ ќЉќµ 3 ќњѕБќЄќ≠ѕВ ќ≥ѕЙќљќѓќµѕВ + ќѓѕГќµѕВ ќ±ѕАќ≠ќљќ±ќљѕДќє ѕАќїќµѕЕѕБќ≠ѕВ (dedup ќЉќµ ќЇќ±ќљќњќљќєќЇѕМ ќЇќїќµќєќіќѓ). ќФќњѕЕќїќµѕНќµќє ќЇќ±ќє ќ≥ќєќ± ѕГѕДѕБќ±ќЉќЉќ≠ќљќ± ќњѕБќЄќњќ≥ѕОќљќєќ±.
- `findEnclosingRectangle(segments, point, tol)` вАФ min-area ќњѕБќЄќњќ≥ѕОќљќєќњ ѕАќњѕЕ ѕАќµѕБќєќ≠ѕЗќµќє ѕДќњ ѕГќЈќЉќµќѓќњ (`isPointInPolygon`).
- `buildWallFillingRect(rect, вА¶)` вАФ ќђќЊќњќљќ±ѕВ ѕГѕДќЈ ќЉќµѕГќњќЇќђќЄќµѕДќњ ѕДѕЙќљ ќЬќХќУќСќЫќ©ќЭ ѕАќїќµѕЕѕБѕОќљ (ќЉќЃќЇќњѕВ = ќЉќµќ≥ќђќїќЈ), `thickness override` = ќЉќєќЇѕБќЃ ѕАќїќµѕЕѕБќђ (sceneвЖТmm). Reuse `buildDefaultWallParams`/`buildWallEntity`.
- `extractLineSegments(entities)` (LINE + ќ±ќЇќЉќ≠ѕВ POLYLINE/LWPOLYLINE) + `pickSegmentAt(point, segs, tol)` вАФ input adapters.

**Design вАФ ќ≠ќљќ± tool, ѕДѕБќѓѕДќњ placement mode.** ќЭќ≠ќњ `ToolType 'wall-in-region'`¬Ј ѕДќњ ќЩќФќЩќЯ `useWallTool` ќ±ѕАќњќЇѕДќђ `placementMode: 'in-region'` (ќЉќЈќіќ≠ќљ ќіќєѕАќїѕМ tool). Click routing ѕАќµѕБќљќђ **raw** worldPoint. ќ§ќ± accumulated picks ѕЖѕЙѕДќѓќґќњќљѕДќ±ќє ѕЙѕВ selection highlight ќЉќ≠ѕГѕЙ ќљќ≠ќњѕЕ `getRegionPickIds()` (ref-backed, post-click accurate)¬Ј commit ќЇќ±ќЄќ±ѕБќѓќґќµќє ѕДќ± picks вЖТ selection clears.

### Phase ¬ЂќСѕАѕМ ѕАќµѕБќѓќ≥ѕБќ±ќЉќЉќ±¬ї (ќ¶0+ќ¶1) вАФ ¬Ђќ§ќњќѓѕЗќњѕВ ќ±ѕАѕМ ѕАќµѕБќѓќ≥ѕБќ±ќЉќЉќ±¬ї *(вЬЕ IMPLEMENTED 2026-06-01)*

**Intent (Giorgio 2026-06-01):** window/box-select ѕАќђќљѕЙ ѕГѕДќєѕВ **ѕАќ±ѕБќµќєќ≠ѕВ** (ѕАќµѕБќєќ≥ѕБќђќЉќЉќ±ѕДќ±) ќµќљѕМѕВ ќіќњќЉќєќЇќњѕН ѕГѕДќњќєѕЗќµќѓќњѕЕ (ќњѕБќЄќњќ≥ѕОќљќєќњ / ќУ / ќ§ / ќ†) вЖТ ѕДќњ ѕГѕНѕГѕДќЈќЉќ± ќ≤ѕБќѓѕГќЇќµќє ѕДќЈќљ ќµќЊѕОѕДќ±ѕДќЈ ѕАќµѕБќѓќЉќµѕДѕБќњ, ќ≤ќ≥ќђќґќµќє **ќЉѕМќљќњ ѕДќњѕЕ ѕДќњ ѕАќђѕЗќњѕВ ќ±ќљќђ ѕГќЇќ≠ќїќњѕВ** ќ±ѕАѕМ ѕДќЈ ќ≥ќµѕЙќЉќµѕДѕБќѓќ±, ќЇќ±ќє ќіќЈќЉќєќњѕЕѕБќ≥ќµќѓ **ќ±ќїѕЕѕГќѓќіќ± ќЊќµѕЗѕЙѕБќєѕГѕДѕОќљ `WallEntity`** ќ±ќљќђ ќµѕЕќЄѕНќ≥ѕБќ±ќЉќЉќњ ѕГќЇќ≠ќїќњѕВ (ќЇќђќЄќµ ѕДќњќѓѕЗќњѕВ = ќіќєќЇѕМ ѕДќњѕЕ host ќЇќњѕЕѕЖѕЙќЉќђѕДѕЙќљ/BOQ¬Ј miter ѕГѕДќєѕВ ќ≥ѕЙќљќѓќµѕВ). ќФѕНќњ builders, ќЇќњќєќљѕМ SSoT (ќњ 2ќњѕВ = ¬Ђќ§ќњќєѕЗќѓќњ ќ±ѕАѕМ ѕАќµѕБќѓќ≥ѕБќ±ќЉќЉќ±¬ї/`ColumnEntity` вЖТ ќ¶ќђѕГќµќєѕВ 2-3 deferred).

**ќ¶0 вАФ ќЇќњќєќљѕМ SSoT ќ≥ќµѕЙќЉќµѕДѕБќѓќ±ѕВ (pure):**
- [x] **NEW** `bim/walls/perimeter-from-faces.ts` вАФ `extractClosedPolygons` (ќЇќїќµќєѕГѕДќђ polyline/rect entities ќ±ѕАќµѕЕќЄќµќѓќ±ѕВ + ќ±ќїѕЕѕГќѓќіѕЙѕГќЈ ќ±ќљќµќЊќђѕБѕДќЈѕДѕЙќљ ќ≥ѕБќ±ќЉќЉѕОќљ ѕГќµ ќЇќ±ќЄќ±ѕБќњѕНѕВ ќ±ѕАќїќњѕНѕВ ќЇѕНќЇќїќњѕЕѕВ) ¬Ј `classifyPerimeter` (rectangle/L/T/U/composite ќ±ѕАѕМ ќЇќњѕБѕЕѕЖќ≠ѕВ+ќ±ќљќ±ќЇќїќ±ѕГѕДќєќЇќ≠ѕВ ќ≥ѕЙќљќѓќµѕВ¬Ј T vs U ќ±ѕАѕМ ќЇѕЕќЇќїќєќЇќЃ ќ±ѕАѕМѕГѕДќ±ѕГќЈ reflex) ¬Ј `decomposeRectilinear` (slab-sweep ѕГќµ ѕДќњѕАќєќЇѕМ ѕАќїќ±ќѓѕГќєќњ ќµѕЕќЄѕЕќ≥ѕБќ±ќЉќЉќєѕГќЉќ≠ќљќњ ќЉќµ ѕДќЈ ќЉќµќ≥ќ±ќїѕНѕДќµѕБќЈ ќ±ќЇќЉќЃ вЖТ ќњѕБќЄќњќ≥ѕОќљќєќ± ѕГќЇќ≠ќїќЈ, area-preserving, ѕГѕДѕБќ±ќЉќЉќ≠ќљќ± ѕГѕЗќЃќЉќ±ѕДќ± OK) ¬Ј `perimeterFacesToRects` orchestrator вЖТ `{ perimeters, rects, ignoredCount }`. Reuse `findRectanglesFromSegments`/`DetectedRectangle` (wall-in-region) + `rectangleCorners` (wall-from-entity, ќµќЊќЃѕЗќЄќЈ) + `isPointInPolygon`.

**Miter (RECOGNITION):** ќіќµќљ ѕАѕБќњѕГѕДќ≠ќЄќЈќЇќµ ќљќ≠ќњѕВ ќЇѕОќіќєќЇќ±ѕВ вАФ ѕДќњ `commitPerimeterFaces` ќЇќ±ќїќµќѓ `onWallCreated` ќ±ќљќђ ѕГќЇќ≠ќїќњѕВ, ќЇќ±ќє ѕДќњ `addWallToScene.computeWallTrims` (SSoT) ќЊќ±ќљќ±-ѕЕѕАќњќїќњќ≥ќѓќґќµќє trims ѕГќµ ќЯќЫќЯ ѕДќњ scene ѕГќµ ќЇќђќЄќµ ќµќєѕГќ±ќ≥ѕЙќ≥ќЃ вЖТ ѕДќњ batch ќЇќїќµќѓќљќµќє ќЉќµ ѕГѕЙѕГѕДѕМ miter/bevel (ѕМѕАѕЙѕВ ќЃќіќЈ ѕДќњ Mode C). BOQ no-double-count: ѕДќ± leg rects **ќіќєќ±ќЉќµѕБќѓќґќњѕЕќљ** ѕДќњ ѕАќњќїѕНќ≥ѕЙќљќњ (slab partition, ќЉќЈќіќ≠ќљ ќµѕАќєќЇќђќїѕЕѕИќЈ) вЖТ ќ£ footprint = ќµќЉќ≤ќ±ќіѕМќљ ѕАќњќїѕЕќ≥ѕОќљќњѕЕ.

**Out of scope / limitations.**
- Loose-line ќЉќЈ-ќњѕБќЄќњќ≥ѕОќљќєќ± loops ѕАќєќђќљќњќљѕДќ±ќє ќЉѕМќљќњ ѕЙѕВ ќЇќ±ќЄќ±ѕБѕМѕВ ќ±ѕАќїѕМѕВ ќЇѕНќЇќїќњѕВ (ќЇќђќЄќµ ќЇѕМќЉќ≤ќњѕВ ќ≤ќ±ќЄќЉќњѕН 2)¬Ј ќЈ ѕДѕЕѕАќєќЇќЃ ќµќѓѕГќњќіќњѕВ = ќХќЭќС ќЇќїќµќєѕГѕДѕМ polyline.
- `composite` (ќ≥ѕЙќљќѓќµѕВ вЙ† 90¬∞) вЖТ ќіќµќљ ќ±ѕАќњѕГѕЕќљѕДќѓќЄќµѕДќ±ќє ѕГќµ rects вЖТ ќ±ќ≥ќљќњќµќѓѕДќ±ќє ќ≥ќєќ± ѕДќњќѓѕЗќњѕЕѕВ (toast ¬Ђќ±ќ≥ќљќњќЃќЄќЈќЇќ±ќљ¬ї). ќУќєќ± ѕДќњќєѕЗќѓќ± ќЯ.ќ£. ѕЙѕВ ќХќЭќС composite `ColumnEntity` вЖТ **ќ¶2+ќ¶3 вЬЕ** (ќљќ≠ќ± `ColumnKind 'U-shape'/'composite'` + ¬Ђќ§ќњќєѕЗќѓќњ ќ±ѕАѕМ ѕАќµѕБќѓќ≥ѕБќ±ќЉќЉќ±¬ї, ќ≤ќї. ѕАќ±ѕБќ±ќЇќђѕДѕЙ).
- рЯФі browser verify ќµќЇќЇѕБќµќЉќµќѓ (ќУ/ќ† box-select вЖТ ќ±ќїѕЕѕГќѓќіќ± ѕДќњќѓѕЗѕЙќљ, miter, hatch, toast¬Ј ќЇќїќєќЇ-ќЉќ≠ѕГќ±).

### Phase ¬ЂќСѕАѕМ ѕАќµѕБќѓќ≥ѕБќ±ќЉќЉќ±¬ї (ќ¶3) вАФ ¬Ђќ§ќњќєѕЗќѓќњ ќ±ѕАѕМ ѕАќµѕБќѓќ≥ѕБќ±ќЉќЉќ±¬ї (Column ќ±ѕАѕМ faces) *(вЬЕ IMPLEMENTED 2026-06-01)*

**Intent (Giorgio):** box-select ѕГѕДќєѕВ **ѕАќ±ѕБќµќєќ≠ѕВ** ќіќњќЉќєќЇќњѕН ѕГѕДќњќєѕЗќµќѓќњѕЕ (ќњѕБќЄќњќ≥ѕОќљќєќњ/ќУ/ќ§/ќ†/ѕГѕНќљќЄќµѕДќњ) вЖТ **ќХќЭќС `ColumnEntity` (ѕДќњќєѕЗќѓќњ ќЯ.ќ£.) ќ±ќљќђ ќЇќїќµќєѕГѕДќЃ ѕАќµѕБќѓќЉќµѕДѕБќњ** вАФ **ќ†ќЯќ§ќХ** ќ±ѕАќњѕГѕНќљќЄќµѕГќЈ ѕГќµ ќЇќњќЉќЉќђѕДќєќ± (Eurocode 8: ѕГѕНќљќЄќµѕДќЈ ѕГѕДќ±ѕДќєќЇќЃ ќїќµќєѕДќњѕЕѕБќ≥ќѓќ± + boundary elements). 2ќњѕВ builder ѕГѕДќњ ќЩќФќЩќЯ ќЇќњќєќљѕМ SSoT `perimeter-from-faces.ts` (mirror ќСќЪќ°ќЩќТќ©ќ£ ѕДќњѕЕ ¬Ђќ§ќњќѓѕЗќњѕВ ќ±ѕАѕМ ѕАќµѕБќѓќ≥ѕБќ±ќЉќЉќ±¬ї).

**Map `shape вЖТ ColumnKind` (ѕГѕНќ≥ќЇќїќєѕГќЈ ќЇќїќђќіќњѕЕ ETABS Section Designer / Revit / Tekla вАФ exact polygon ќ≥ќєќ± ќЉќЈ-ќњѕБќЄќњќ≥ѕЙќљќєќЇќђ):**
- `rectangle` вЖТ `rectangular` (ќЃ `shear-wall` ќ±ќљ aspect вЙ• `SHEAR_WALL_MIN_ASPECT_RATIO`=4) вАФ **ќ†ќСќ°ќСќЬќХќ§ќ°ќЩќЪќЯ** (width=longSide, depth=shortSide, rotation=ќ≥ѕЙќљќѓќ± ќЉќµќ≥ќђќїќЈѕВ ќ±ќЇќЉќЃѕВ).
- `L` / `T` / `composite` вЖТ `composite` вАФ **POLYGON-BACKED** (ќ±ќЇѕБќєќ≤ќ≠ѕВ ѕАќњќїѕНќ≥ѕЙќљќњ).
- `U` (ќ†) вЖТ `U-shape` вАФ **POLYGON-BACKED** (`ushape.polygon`).

**polygon-centering (ќЈ geometry pipeline ѕДќњ ќµќЉѕАќєѕГѕДќµѕНќµѕДќ±ќє):** ѕДќњ polygon ќ±ѕАќњќЄќЈќЇќµѕНќµѕДќ±ќє LOCAL mm, bbox-centered, CCW¬Ј `position`=bbox-center world, `anchor`='center', `rotation`=0 вЖТ `transformFootprint` (anchor center вЖТ ќЉќЈќіќ≠ќљ shift) ќЊќ±ќљќ±ќ≥ѕЕѕБќљќђ ќСќЪќ°ќЩќТќ©ќ£ ѕГѕДќњ ќ±ѕБѕЗќєќЇѕМ world ѕАќµѕБќѓќ≥ѕБќ±ќЉќЉќ± (round-trip test).

**Files:**
- [x] **NEW** `bim/columns/column-from-faces.ts` вАФ `perimeterFacesToColumns(entities, tol, layerId, sceneUnits)` + `buildColumnsFromPerimeters(perimeters, вА¶)` (click-inside path). Reuse `perimeterFacesToRects`/`classifyPerimeter` (ќЯќІќЩ `decomposeRectilinear` вАФ ќХќЭќС entity) + `completeColumnFromClick` (params+validation+geometry SSoT). Helpers `polygonBbox`/`polygonToLocalMm`/`rectColumnPlacement`/`polygonColumnPlacement`.
- [x] `hooks/drawing/column-completion.ts` вАФ `ColumnParamOverrides` + `buildDefaultColumnParams` ќµѕАќµќЇѕДќђќЄќЈќЇќ±ќљ ќЉќµ `ushape`/`composite` (ќ≠ќїќµќєѕАќµ ѕДќњ override path ѕДќЈѕВ ќ¶2 вАФ ѕДѕОѕБќ± SSoT-complete, ѕЗѕБќЃѕГќєќЉќњ ќЇќ±ќє ќ≥ќєќ± ќ¶2b manual creation).

- [x] `hooks/tools/useSpecialTools.ts` вАФ column lifecycle ѕГќµ `'column'||'column-from-perimeter'` + `setPlacementMode` ќ±ќљќђ tool + `getSceneEntities`.
- [x] Tool `'column-from-perimeter'`: `ui/toolbar/types.ts` + `systems/tools/tool-definitions.ts` (drawing, continuous) + `ui/ribbon/data/home-tab-draw.ts` (`draw.bim.columnFromPerimeter`) + `app/ribbon-contextual-config.ts` (shares column contextual tab) + 4 box-select gates (`useCentralizedMouseHandlers`/`mouse-handler-move`/`-up`/`useCanvasClickHandler`/`dxf-canvas-renderer`).

- [x] **NEW** `bim/columns/__tests__/column-from-faces.test.ts` (9: rectвЖТrectangular, ќЉќ±ќЇѕБѕМѕГѕДќµќљќњвЖТshear-wall, ќУ/ќ§/ѕГѕДќ±ѕЕѕБѕМѕВвЖТcomposite, ќ†вЖТU-shape, round-trip footprint, ќХќЭќС entity/ѕАќµѕБќѓќЉќµѕДѕБќњ, bowtieвЖТignored). **14/14** ќ¶3+wall-from-perimeter regression¬Ј **578/578** column suites¬Ј tsc clean.

**Insertion (RECOGNITION):** ѕМѕАѕЙѕВ ќњќє ѕДќњќѓѕЗќњќє, ќњќє ќЇќњќїѕОќљќµѕВ ќФќХќЭ ќ≠ѕЗќњѕЕќљ undo-command вАФ per-entity append ќЉќ≠ѕГѕЙ `onColumnCreated` вЖТ `addColumnToScene` (broadcast `drawing:entity-created`). ќФќµќљ ѕАѕБќњѕГѕДќ≠ќЄќЈќЇќµ command (ѕДќњ checklist ¬ЂAddColumnsFromFacesCommand¬ї ќ±ѕЖќњѕБќњѕНѕГќµ ќ±ќљѕНѕАќ±ѕБќЇѕДќњ command).

**Deferred:** ќ¶2b (interactive resize grips U-shape + mirror flipY + section-profile steel symbols + panel kind-picker). рЯФі browser verify (ќУ/ќ†/ѕГѕДќ±ѕЕѕБѕМѕВ box-select вЖТ ќХќЭќС ѕДќњќєѕЗќѓќњ/ѕАќµѕБќѓќЉќµѕДѕБќњ, ѕГѕЙѕГѕДќЃ ќ≥ќµѕЙќЉќµѕДѕБќѓќ±, column contextual ribbon, toast).

### Phase 2 вАФ Opening *(вЬЕ CORE IMPLEMENTED 2026-05-18)*

**Files added (Phase 2 core):**
- `bim/types/opening-types.ts` вАФ 5 kinds (door/window/sliding-door/french-door/fixed), `OpeningParams`/`OpeningGeometry`/`OpeningEntity` concrete types, `OPENING_KIND_DEFAULTS` per-kind defaults, `OPENING_SNAP_INCREMENT_MM` (50mm).
- `bim/geometry/opening-geometry.ts` вАФ `computeOpeningGeometry(params, hostWall)` pure SSoT (outline rect on axis, `position`/`rotation`/`bbox`/`area`(m¬≤)/`perimeter`(m)), `projectPointToWallOffset()` helper for snap-to-host.
- `bim/validators/opening-validator.ts` вАФ `validateOpeningParams(params, hostWall)` вАФ hard errors (`missingHostWall`, `widthTooSmall`, `heightTooSmall`, `offsetNegative`, `sillNegative`, `overflowsHostLength`, `overflowsHostHeight`) + code violations (`widthExceedsThicknessRatio`, `doorWithSill`).
- `hooks/drawing/opening-completion.ts` вАФ `buildDefaultOpeningParams` + `buildOpeningEntity` + `completeOpeningFromHostClick` (pure builders, generateOpeningId via N.6).
- `hooks/drawing/useOpeningTool.ts` вАФ FSM `idle вЖТ awaitingHostWall вЖТ awaitingPosition вЖТ committed`, continuous-draw chain, ESC handling, status text i18n keys.
- `bim/walls/opening-firestore-service.ts` вАФ `OpeningFirestoreService` + `OpeningDoc` (mirror `WallFirestoreService`).
- `hooks/data/useOpeningPersistence.ts` вАФ 500ms auto-save debounce, diff-merge, first-save listener, delete-requested listener, geometry re-derive from `params + hostWall` on hydrate.
- `bim/walls/opening-audit-client.ts` вАФ fire-and-forget `recordOpeningChange()` (ADR-195 endpoint).
- `bim/renderers/OpeningRenderer.ts` вАФ outline + hinge arc (door/french-door) + glazing inset (window/fixed/french-door) + sliding-door track indicator.
- `ui/ribbon/data/contextual-opening-tab.ts` + `ui/ribbon/hooks/bridge/opening-command-keys.ts` + `ui/ribbon/hooks/useRibbonOpeningBridge.ts` вАФ Kind / Size / Actions panels ќЉќµ close + delete buttons.
- `app/OpeningPersistenceHost.tsx` вАФ always-on hook host (mounted by `DxfViewerTopBar`).

**Files modified (Phase 2 wiring):**
- `types/audit-trail.ts` вАФ `AuditEntityType` += `'opening'`.

- `hooks/tools/useSpecialTools.ts` вАФ `useOpeningTool` wired with `getWallById` / `getWallAtPoint` resolvers + bbox-based host lookup; `onOpeningCreated` syncs `hostedOpeningIds` mirror on the host wall and emits `drawing:entity-created`.
- `ui/ribbon/hooks/useRibbonCommands.ts` вАФ composer wires `openingBridge` for combobox / state / action / badge keys.

**Tests added (26+):**
- `bim/geometry/__tests__/opening-geometry.test.ts` вАФ outline shape, center positioning, rotation (horizontal/vertical), area (m¬≤), perimeter (m), bbox folding, hinge arc presence per kind, french-door dual-arc, `projectPointToWallOffset` clamping (15 tests).

**Phase 2.5 вАФ Opening Advanced Editing (вЬЕ IMPLEMENTED 2026-05-18):**
- [x] **`UpdateOpeningParamsCommand`** вАФ `core/commands/entity-commands/UpdateOpeningParamsCommand.ts`. Atomic params + geometry + validation patch with merge window (ADR-031). Soft-orphan tolerant: missing host wall вЖТ intrinsic validation only, geometry preserved.
- [x] **Drag-along-wall grip** вАФ `bim/walls/opening-grips.ts` (pure). Single `opening-offset` grip; `applyOpeningGripDrag()` projects cursor onto host wall axis and clamps to `[frameWidth, hostLength - width - frameWidth]` so the cutout always retains a minimum jamb on each side.
- [x] **`openingGripKind` discriminator** вАФ added to `hooks/grip-types.ts` (`GripInfo`) + `hooks/grips/unified-grip-types.ts` (`UnifiedGripInfo`); forwarded by `grip-registry.wrapDxfGrip()` so the unified pipeline carries the kind through to commit.
- [x] **`commitOpeningGripDrag`** вАФ new case in `hooks/grips/grip-commit-adapters.ts`; routed by `commitDxfGripDragModeAware` ahead of stretch/move strategies. Emits `bim:opening-params-updated` after dispatch.
- [x] **`OpeningRenderer.getGrips`** вАФ wired to `getOpeningGrips()` (replaces Phase 2 stub returning `[]`).
- [x] **Ribbon bridge refactor** вАФ `ui/ribbon/hooks/useRibbonOpeningBridge.ts` dispatches every mutation through `UpdateOpeningParamsCommand` (via `useCommandHistory().execute`) so ribbon edits are undoable, mirroring the wall bridge pattern.
- [x] **Boolean cutout on wall fill** вАФ `bim/renderers/WallRenderer.ts` accepts a per-frame `OpeningsByWall` map (`setOpeningsByWall()`); subtracts each hosted opening outline from the wall fill via `globalCompositeOperation='destination-out'`, scoped by `save/restore`. `EntityRendererComposite.setOpeningsByWall()` forwards from the canvas pipeline. ADR-040 micro-leaf compliant (renderer never subscribes вАФ caller pushes per-frame map).

**Tests added Phase 2.5 (3 suites):**
- `bim/walls/__tests__/opening-grips.test.ts` вАФ 8 tests: grip layout, axis projection, clamp min/max, refuse on undersized host, idempotent identity, foreign grip kind no-op.
- `core/commands/entity-commands/__tests__/UpdateOpeningParamsCommand.test.ts` вАФ 11 tests: execute/undo/redo, merge window (same opening, both dragging), validator rejects, soft-orphan host-missing path, serialize round-trip.
- `bim/renderers/__tests__/WallRenderer-with-openings.test.ts` вАФ 6 tests: cutout pass scoping (save/restore), `destination-out` only when openings registered, foreign-wall openings ignored, stroke survives cutout, multi-opening punching.

- [x] Wall delete prompt "ќФќєќ±ќ≥ѕБќ±ѕЖќЃ ќЇќ±ќє ѕДѕЙќљ N ќЇќњѕЕѕЖѕЙќЉќђѕДѕЙќљ;" (cascading delete UX). **вЖТ Phase cascade-delete (2026-05-19)**: `WallCascadeDeleteDialog` + `wall-cascade-delete-store`.
- [x] Hotkey `OP` (Opening 2-char chord) вАФ **implemented Phase 7A** (2026-05-18) via `MultiCharKeySequence`. `O` alone вЖТ `tool:layering` (fallback, toggle), `OP` вЖТ `tool:opening`.
- [x] Single-char variant shortcuts `D`/`Wn` вАФ **implemented Phase 7B (2026-05-19)** via EventBus. `D` (context-sensitive when `activeTool === 'opening'`) вЖТ `bim:set-opening-kind` вЖТ kind=`'door'`. `W+1/2/3` BIM chords вЖТ `bim:set-wall-kind` вЖТ kind=`'straight'/'curved'/'polyline'` + `onToolChange('wall')`. `W` alone вЖТ fallback `tool:wall` (unchanged). `D` outside opening context вЖТ falls through to `measureDistance` (no conflict).
- [x] Polyline / curved host wall positioning вАФ **Phase 2 leftover (2026-05-20)**: `getWallAxisVertices()` + `walkPolylineToDistance()` + `projectPointToPolylineOffset()`. (Originally via `WallOpeningCoordinator`; since 2026-05-29 ¬І5.4 the cascade uses `computeOpeningGeometry` directly вАФ same arc-length walk.) 11 new tests.
- [x] Canvas pipeline call site for `composite.setOpeningsByWall(...)` вАФ **implemented Phase 2 deferred (2026-05-19)**. `DxfOpening` wrapper added to `dxf-types.ts`; `case 'opening'` added to `useDxfSceneConversion.ts` and `DxfRenderer.toEntityModel()`; `DxfRenderer.buildOpeningsByWall()` builds `Map<wallId, OpeningEntity[]>` per-frame from scene entities; `DxfRenderer.render()` calls `composite.setOpeningsByWall(map)` before the entity render pass вАФ WallRenderer now punches boolean cutouts through wall fills for all hosted openings.
- [x] **Opening tool canvas wiring + ghost preview + scene-units thread вАФ implemented 2026-05-25 canvas-wiring follow-up.** Silent failure resolved: `useCanvasClickHandler` now dispatches `worldPoint вЖТ openingTool.onCanvasClick` (new PRIORITY 4.96 branch, mirrors slab-opening PRIORITY 4.95); new `useOpeningGhostPreview` hook + `OpeningGhostRenderer` (dashed rectangle + crosshair + per-kind palette + optional hinge arc) + `OpeningGhostPreviewMount` micro-leaf mounted in `PreviewCanvasMounts`; `CanvasSection.tsx` destructures `openingTool` from `useSpecialTools` (previously dropped) and feeds the `openingGhostPreview` payload with a `getHostWall` resolver; `buildDefaultOpeningParams` + `buildOpeningEntity` + `computeOpeningGeometry` gain an optional `sceneUnits: SceneUnits = 'mm'` parameter so the projected offset stays in mm (per `OpeningParams` contract) and the outline scales correctly for scene='m'/'cm'/'in'/'ft'; `useOpeningTool` accepts an optional `getSceneUnits` resolver, wired by `useSpecialTools` via `resolveSceneUnits(level scene)`. ADR-040 micro-leaf compliance preserved (ghost subscribes to `useCursorWorldPosition` internally; CanvasSection / CanvasLayerStack don't re-render on mousemove). Pre-existing scene-unit drift in the edit paths (`computeOpeningGeometry` callers from grip-commit / move / mirror / rotate / cascade) carries over as a separate follow-up. **вЖТ RESOLVED (2026-05-29, ¬І5.4 unified cascade)**: `cascadeHostedOpeningsForWalls` reads `sceneUnits` ќ±ѕАѕМ `wall.params.sceneUnits ?? 'mm'` ѕГќµ ќЯќЫќС ѕДќ± transform/param paths (meter-scene safe, ADR-397/398).

- [x] i18n (el+en) + 3 test suites (slab-geometry, slab-validator, useSlabTool).
- [x] ¬І5.5 schema realized via concrete types in `bim/types/slab-types.ts` (replaced Phase 0 stub).
- [x] Hotkey `SL` (Slab 2-char chord) вАФ **implemented Phase 7A** (2026-05-18) via `MultiCharKeySequence`. `S` alone вЖТ `tool:select` (fallback), `S+T` вЖТ stair, `S+L` вЖТ slab.

**Phase 3.5 вАФ Slab Advanced Editing (вЬЕ IMPLEMENTED 2026-05-18):**
- [x] **`UpdateSlabParamsCommand`** вАФ `core/commands/entity-commands/UpdateSlabParamsCommand.ts`. Atomic params + geometry + validation patch with merge window (ADR-031). Root `kind` synced with `params.kind` so the ribbon's kind switch remains undoable.
- [x] **Per-vertex polygon grip** вАФ `bim/slabs/slab-grips.ts` (pure). `slab-vertex-N` family (one grip per outline vertex); `applySlabGripDrag()` translates the indexed vertex by `delta` (XY only, z preserved). Edge-midpoint vertex insertion deferred to Phase 3.6.
- [x] **`slabGripKind` discriminator** вАФ added to `hooks/grip-types.ts` (`GripInfo`) + re-exported from `hooks/useGripMovement.ts` + `hooks/grips/unified-grip-types.ts` (`UnifiedGripInfo`); forwarded by `grip-registry.wrapDxfGrip()` so the unified pipeline carries the kind through to commit.
- [x] **`commitSlabGripDrag`** вАФ new case in `hooks/grips/grip-commit-adapters.ts`; routed by `commitDxfGripDragModeAware` ahead of stretch/move strategies. Emits `bim:slab-params-updated` after dispatch.
- [x] **`SlabRenderer.getGrips`** вАФ wired to `getSlabGrips()` (replaces Phase 3 stub returning `[]`).
- [x] **Ribbon bridge refactor** вАФ `ui/ribbon/hooks/useRibbonSlabBridge.ts` dispatches every mutation through `UpdateSlabParamsCommand` (via `useCommandHistory().execute` + `LevelSceneManagerAdapter`) so ribbon edits are undoable, mirroring the wall / opening bridge pattern. Direct scene patch + `computeSlabGeometry` / `validateSlabParams` calls removed (those now happen inside the command).

**Tests added Phase 3.5 (2 suites):**
- `bim/slabs/__tests__/slab-grips.test.ts` вАФ 10 tests: grip layout per outline vertex, stable index order, type/movesEntity invariants, degenerate-polygon empty list, per-index drag translation, z preservation, zero-delta + out-of-range short-circuit, unknown-grip-kind no-op.
- `core/commands/entity-commands/__tests__/UpdateSlabParamsCommand.test.ts` вАФ 12 tests: execute/undo/redo round-trip, geometry recompute (4√Ч3 вЖТ 5√Ч3 m¬≤ rectangle), root-kind sync with `params.kind`, undo-before-execute no-op, merge window (same slab + both dragging + within window), foreign-slab merge guard, validator rejects empty id / degenerate outline / non-positive thickness, serialize round-trip.

**Deferred to Phase 3.6+ (Phase 3.5 close-out list):**
- [x] Edge-midpoint vertex insertion (`slab-edge-midpoint-N` grip вЖТ adds a new vertex at the edge midpoint). **Done Phase 3.6.**
- [x] Slab-opening separate entity (¬І11.Q3) + boolean cutout on slab fill (mirrors wall's `OpeningsByWall` pattern from Phase 2.5). **Done Phase 3.7.**
- [x] Rectilinear constraint (Shift toggle clamps grip drag to dominant world axis). **Done Phase 3.6.**
- [x] Hatch patterns per `reinforcement` (one-way / two-way / waffle / flat). **Done Phase 3.6.**
- [x] maxFreeSpan analytical (1D beam-direction span detection вАФ currently crude bbox max-dimension). **вЬЕ Phase 3.8 (2026-05-20)**.

**Phase 3.6 вАФ Slab Polish (вЬЕ IMPLEMENTED 2026-05-18):**
- [x] **Edge-midpoint vertex insertion** вАФ `bim/slabs/slab-grips.ts` extended. `getSlabGrips()` now returns `2N` grips for an `N`-vertex polygon: indices `[0, N)` are vertex grips (`slab-vertex-N`, Phase 3.5 behaviour preserved) and indices `[N, 2N)` are edge-midpoint grips (`slab-edge-midpoint-N`) anchored at `midpoint(verts[N], verts[(N+1) mod len])`. `applySlabGripDrag('slab-edge-midpoint-N', вА¶)` splits edge `[N, N+1]` by inserting a fresh vertex at `midpoint + delta`; z is averaged from the two endpoints when present.
- [x] **Rectilinear (Shift) constraint** вАФ `SlabGripDragInput.rectilinear?: boolean`. When `true`, `applySlabGripDrag` quantizes `delta` to the dominant world axis (`|dx| вЙ• |dy|` вЖТ keep dx, drop dy; otherwise reverse). Applies to both vertex translate and edge-midpoint insertion.
- [x] **`ShiftKeyTracker`** вАФ new singleton in `src/subapps/dxf-viewer/keyboard/ShiftKeyTracker.ts`. Vanilla pub/sub mirror of `GripCopyModeStore`; installs `window` `keydown`/`keyup`/`blur` listeners once at module load (SSR-safe). Exposes `getSnapshot()` for commit-time consumers that cannot plumb the modifier through `useUnifiedGripInteraction.handleMouseUp(worldPos)` (which intentionally drops the native event). ADR-040 compliant вАФ low-frequency UI events, no render-path subscriptions.
- [x] **`commitSlabGripDrag` reads tracker** вАФ `hooks/grips/grip-parametric-commits.ts` passes `rectilinear: ShiftKeyTracker.getSnapshot()` into `applySlabGripDrag`. No signature change to `commitDxfGripDragModeAware`/`DxfCommitDeps`.
- [x] **`SlabGripKind` discriminator extended** вАФ `hooks/grip-types.ts` now declares the discriminated union `slab-vertex-${number} | slab-edge-midpoint-${number}`. Re-exports through `hooks/useGripMovement.ts` + `hooks/grips/unified-grip-types.ts` propagate automatically.
- [x] **Reinforcement hatch in `SlabRenderer`** вАФ new private `drawReinforcementHatch(slab)` pass runs between fill and stroke when `params.reinforcement` is set. Polygon-clipped (save вЖТ polygon path вЖТ clip вЖТ hatch вЖТ restore). World-space spacing per family: one-way 200mm horizontal, two-way 300mm orthogonal grid, waffle 150mm dense cross-hatch, flat 250mm dot grid. Stroke kept faint (`rgba(0,0,0,0.15)`, `lineWidth=0.5`) so the outline + fill stay readable. Industry convention (Revit/ArchiCAD plan-view hint hatch).
- [x] **`SlabRenderer.getGrips` carries midpoint type** вАФ vertex grips render as `type: 'vertex'`, edge midpoints as `type: 'midpoint'` (already in `rendering/types/Types.ts` `GripInfo['type']` union).

**Tests added Phase 3.6 (1 suite + 10 new tests):**
- `bim/slabs/__tests__/slab-grips.test.ts` вАФ extended to 20 tests: existing 10 Phase 3.5 tests retained (covering vertex layout + drag translation + z preservation + zero-delta / out-of-range / unknown short-circuit) + 10 new Phase 3.6 tests covering edge-midpoint grip positions (incl. closing edge wrap), `type='midpoint'` + `edgeVertexIndices`, vertex insertion at `midpoint + delta` (length+1, original vertices untouched), out-of-range edge index short-circuit, rectilinear quantization on each axis tie-break, edge-midpoint + rectilinear interaction, and `rectilinear=false` default preserves full delta.
- `bim/renderers/__tests__/SlabRenderer-hatch.test.ts` вАФ 7 canvas-mock tests (firebase/auth stubbed): no reinforcement вЖТ no `clip` call, one-way вЖТ clip + horizontal hatch lines only, two-way > one-way line count, waffle > two-way density, flat вЖТ arc/fill dot grid (no parallel-line strokes), scoped save/clip/restore, stroke survives clip.

**Deferred to Phase 3.7+:**
- [x] Slab-opening separate entity (¬І11.Q3) + boolean cutout on slab fill (mirrors wall's `OpeningsByWall` pattern from Phase 2.5). **Done Phase 3.7.**
- [x] maxFreeSpan analytical (1D beam-direction span detection). **вЬЕ Phase 3.8 (2026-05-20).**
- [ ] Per-material hatch palette (Phase 6+ depends on material library).
- [x] ~~Snap-to-edge-midpoint preview ghost while hovering edge midpoint grip pre-drag.~~ **вЬЕ Phase 3.7b++ (2026-05-20)**: green "+vertex" indicator at `hoveredEdgeMidpointGrip.position` via `useSlabOpeningGhostPreview` extension.

### Phase 3.7 вАФ Slab-Opening Entity *(вЬЕ IMPLEMENTED 2026-05-18)*

### Phase 3.7c вАФ Slab-Opening visibility fix (z-order + scene-units) *(вЬЕ IMPLEMENTED 2026-05-25)*

**Bug**: User ѕГѕЗќµќіќѓќ±ќґќµ slab-opening ѕАќђќљѕЙ ѕГќµ ѕАќїќђќЇќ± ѕГѕДќњ `/dxf/viewer` ќ±ќїќїќђ ќЇќ±ќЉќѓќ± ќњѕАќЃ ќіќµќљ ќµќЉѕЖќ±ќљќєќґѕМѕДќ±ќљ вАФ ќњѕНѕДќµ ghost preview, ќњѕНѕДќµ committed entity.

**Two independent root causes**:

1. **Scene-units bug** (size off by 1000√Ч): ќњ `buildDefaultSlabOpeningParams` ѕАќ±ќѓѕБќљќµќє `widthMm: 1500` ќ±ќїќїќђ ѕДќ± ќ≠ќ≤ќ±ќґќµ ѕГѕДќњ polygon ќІќ©ќ°ќЩќ£ conversion ѕГѕДќєѕВ scene units вЖТ ѕГќµ scene ѕГќµ `'m'`, rectangle ќ≠ќ≤ќ≥ќ±ќєќљќµ 1500√Ч1500 m ќ±ќљѕДќѓ 1.5√Ч1.5 m, totally outside slab. Mirror ѕДќњѕЕ slab-completion Phase 8 fix.
   - Fix: propagation `sceneUnits` field ѕГќµ `SlabOpeningParams`, `mmToSceneUnits()` factor ќµѕЖќ±ѕБќЉќњќ≥ќЃ ќ†ќ°ќЩќЭ ѕДќњ polygon build, area calc ќЉќµ `canvasToM` conversion.
   - Files: `bim/types/slab-opening-types.ts` (+`sceneUnits` field), `bim/geometry/slab-opening-geometry.ts` (canvasToM), `bim/validators/slab-opening-validator.ts` (area conversion), `hooks/drawing/slab-opening-completion.ts` (mmвЖТscene), `hooks/tools/useSpecialTools-slab-opening.ts` (getSceneUnits via resolveSceneUnits).
   - Ghost preview parity: `useSlabOpeningGhostPreview.ts` + `canvas-layer-stack-slab-opening-ghost.tsx` (passthrough `getSceneUnits` prop), `components/dxf-layout/CanvasSection.tsx` (wire `resolveSceneUnits` вЖТ `slabOpeningGhostPreview`).

2. **Z-order bug** (rendered but invisible): ќњќє 5+ persisted slab-openings ќ±ѕАѕМ Firestore ќ≠ѕБѕЗќњќљѕДќ±ќљ ѕГѕДќњ `scene.entities` array ќ†ќ°ќЩќЭ ѕДќ± persisted slabs (snapshot delivery order). ќЯ `DxfRenderer` iterate-ќµќє sequentially вЖТ openings ќґѕЙќ≥ѕБќ±ѕЖќѓќґќњќљѕДќ±ќљ ѕАѕБѕОѕДќ±, slabs ќЬќХќ§ќС ќ†ќСќЭќ© ѕДќњѕЕѕВ (alpha-blend 20%). ќ§ќњ `punchHostedSlabOpenings` ќЉќµ `destination-out` ќ≠ѕГќ≤ќЈќљќµ ќЪќСќЩ ѕДќ± slab ќЪќСќЩ ѕДќ± opening pixels ѕГѕДќњ cutout area вЖТ ќ±ѕМѕБќ±ѕДќЈ ќњѕАќЃ.
   - Fix: **two-pass rendering** ѕГѕДќњ `DxfRenderer.ts` per-entity loop:
     - Pass A: ѕМќїќ± ѕДќ± entities ќХќЪќ§ќЯќ£ slab-opening (slab fill + `punchHostedSlabOpenings` ќЉќµ destination-out clears cutout).
     - Pass B: ќЉѕМќљќњ slab-openings (dashed outline + kind fill ќ†ќСќЭќ© ќ±ѕАѕМ slab).
   - Industry parallel: AutoCAD/Revit z-order вАФ structural cutouts always rendered on top of host element ќ≥ќєќ± ќљќ± ќЉќЈ ѕЗќђќљќњќљѕДќ±ќє ѕГќµ alpha-blend.
   - Files: `canvas-v2/dxf-canvas/DxfRenderer.ts` (two-pass loop), `bim/renderers/SlabOpeningRenderer.ts` (visual enhancement: KIND_STROKE darker/more saturated, KIND_FILL alpha 0.35 ќ±ѕАѕМ 0.18, lineWidth `THICK` 3px ќ±ѕАѕМ `NORMAL` 2px).
   - **Preventive note**: ќКќіќєќњ pattern ќЉѕАќњѕБќµќѓ ќљќ± ѕЗѕБќµќєќ±ѕГѕДќµќѓ preventively ѕГќµ `opening` (window/door) vs `wall` ќ±ќљ ќµќЉѕЖќ±ќљќєѕГѕДќµќѓ. WallRenderer ѕЗѕБќЈѕГќєќЉќњѕАќњќєќµќѓ identical `punchHostedOpenings` ќЉќµ destination-out вАФ ќѓќіќєќњ risk.

**Verification**: Magenta debug stroke ќµѕАќєќ≤ќµќ≤ќ±ќѓѕЙѕГќµ render path ѕАѕБќєќљ cleanup. User confirmed ќњѕАѕДќєќЇќђ ѕМѕДќє ќњќє 9 ѕЕѕАќђѕБѕЗќњѕЕѕГќµѕВ ќњѕАќ≠ѕВ ќµќЉѕЖќ±ќљќѓѕГѕДќЈќЇќ±ќљ ќЉќµѕДќђ ѕДќњ fix.

### Phase 3.7d вАФ Slab-Opening 3D coverage parity *(вЬЕ IMPLEMENTED 2026-05-25)*

Cross-reference: ADR-370 ¬І6 Phase 7 changelog (read-only 3D + `/dxf/viewer` toggle).

**Bug**: ќЉќµѕДќђ ѕДќЈќљ Phase 3.7c (2D visibility), ќњќє ќњѕАќ≠ѕВ ќµќЉѕЖќ±ќљќѓќґќњќљѕДќ±ќљ ѕГѕЙѕГѕДќђ ѕГѕДќњ 2D `/dxf/viewer` ќ±ќїќїќђ ќњќє BIM ѕАќїќђќЇќµѕВ ѕГќµ 3D (toggle 3D ѕГѕДќњ `/dxf/viewer` ќЪќСќЩ Properties read-only 3D ѕГќµ `?view=floorplan&mediaTab=floorplan-floor`) ќµќЉѕЖќ±ќљќѓќґќњќљѕДќ±ќљ solid ѕЗѕЙѕБќѓѕВ cutouts. Mirror gap ѕДќЈѕВ Phase 5 stair coverage.

**Root cause**: `Bim3DEntities` interface ќіќµќљ ќµќѓѕЗќµ `slabOpenings` field, `slabToMesh` ќіќµќљ ќіќµѕЗѕМѕДќ±ќљ openings array, `BimSceneLayer.sync` ќіќµќљ ѕДќ± ѕАќ≠ѕБќљќ±ќ≥ќµ ѕГѕДќњ converter, `Bim3DReadOnlyOverlay` ќіќµќљ ѕДќ± forwardќђѕБќµќє ќ±ѕАѕМ ѕДќњ `useFloorplanBimEntities` snapshot.

**Industry-standard fix** (`THREE.Shape.holes` + `ExtrudeGeometry` native ear-clipping triangulation, mirror IFC `IfcRelVoidsElement` voiding `IfcSlab` / Revit Floor+Opening family / AutoCAD ARCHITECTURE Slab+Opening pattern):

- [x] `bim-3d/stores/Bim3DEntitiesStore.ts` вАФ `slabOpenings: readonly SlabOpeningEntity[]` field + `setSlabOpenings(arr)` setter + `selectBim3DEntities` includes slabOpenings.
- [x] `bim-3d/converters/BimToThreeConverter.ts` вАФ `slabToMesh(slab, openings=[], levelId?, buildingBaseElevationM?)`. ќЭќ≠ќњѕВ helper `pushHoles(shape, openings)` ѕАќњѕЕ reverses vertex winding (BIM CCW вЖТ THREE.Path CW) ѕАѕБќєќљ push ѕГѕДќњ `shape.holes`. `ExtrudeGeometry` handles triangulation natively. Hole inherits slab extrude z (no override вАФ `elevationOverride` field reserved ќ≥ќєќ± future multi-storey stack visualization).
- [x] `bim-3d/scene/BimSceneLayer.ts` вАФ slab loop: filter `entities.slabOpenings.filter(o => o.params.slabId === slab.id)`, pass ѕЙѕВ 2ќњ arg ѕГѕДќњ `slabToMesh`. Inline (no separate loop) ќ≥ќєќ±ѕДќѓ openings ќµќѓќљќ±ќє attachments ѕГѕДќњ host slab вАФ ќґѕЙќ≥ѕБќ±ѕЖќѓќґќњќљѕДќ±ќє ќЉќ±ќґќѓ ѕГѕДќњ extrude.
- [x] `bim-3d/viewport/BimViewport3D.tsx` вАФ `EMPTY_BIM_ENTITIES.slabOpenings = []` + initial sync destructuring + ongoing subscribe pushes `s.slabOpenings`.
- [x] `components/shared/files/media/Bim3DReadOnlyOverlay.tsx` вАФ `useMemo` deps + `slabOpenings: bimSnapshot.slabOpenings`. (`useFloorplanBimEntities` ќЃќіќЈ subscribed ѕГќµ `FLOORPLAN_SLAB_OPENINGS` ќ±ѕАѕМ ADR-370 Phase 1 вАФ ќЉѕМќљќњ forwarding ѕЗѕБќµќєќ±ќґѕМѕДќ±ќљ.)
- [x] `app/SlabOpeningPersistenceHost.tsx` вАФ `+useEffect` ѕАќњѕЕ ѕАќєќ≠ќґќµќє `currentScene.entities.filter(isSlabOpeningEntity)` ѕГѕДќњ `Bim3DEntitiesStore.setSlabOpenings()`. Mirror `SlabPersistenceHost` lines 58-61. `SlabOpeningPersistenceHost` ѕЕѕАќЃѕБѕЗќµ ќЃќіќЈ ќ±ѕАѕМ Phase 3.7 (Firestore persistence) вАФ ќЉѕМќљќњ additive 3D feed hookup, ќЇќ±ќЉќѓќ± ќљќ≠ќ± ѕЖќєќїќњќЊќµќљќњѕНќЉќµќљќЈ responsibility.

**Multi-storey stack**: groups (`SlabOpeningStackHost` Phase 3.7b+) ќіќњѕЕќїќµѕНќњѕЕќљ ќ±ѕЕѕДѕМќЉќ±ѕДќ± вАФ ќЇќђќЄќµ floor ќ≠ѕЗќµќє own slab + own opening doc, ќњ `slabId` filter cuts per-floor ѕЗѕЙѕБќѓѕВ ќµќєќіќєќЇѕМ handling.

**Performance**: CHECK 6B/6C compliant (ѕМќїќµѕВ ќ±ќїќїќ±ќ≥ќ≠ѕВ low-frequency вАФ user-triggered entity changes). Per-slab opening filter ќµќѓќљќ±ќє O(N√ЧM) ѕМѕАќњѕЕ N=slabs, M=openings. ќУќєќ± typical project (~20 slabs √Ч ~5 openings = 100 ops/rebuild) ќіќµќљ ѕАќ±ѕБќ±ѕДќЈѕБќµќѓѕДќ±ќє FPS regression. Phase 3+ incremental dirty-tracking ќЄќ± optimize ќ±ќљ ѕЗѕБќµќєќ±ѕГѕДќµќѓ.

**No Firestore touch**: ZERO writes вАФ ќЉѕМќљќњ 3D pipeline read-side. Schema, rules, indexes ќ±ќЉќµѕДќђќ≤ќїќЈѕДќ± ќ±ѕАѕМ Phase 3.7c.

### Phase 3.7a вАФ Slab-Opening Grips *(вЬЕ IMPLEMENTED 2026-05-18)*

Closes the Phase 3.7 deferred list for slab-opening editing affordances. Mirrors
ќ±ќЇѕБќєќ≤ѕОѕВ ѕДќњ Phase 3.5/3.6 pattern ѕДќњѕЕ slab (per-vertex translate + edge-midpoint
vertex insertion + Shift-rectilinear quantization).

- [x] `bim/slab-openings/slab-opening-grips.ts` вАФ pure handlers (zero React /
  DOM / Firestore / canvas deps): `getSlabOpeningGrips(entity)` returns `2N`
  grips (`[0, N)` vertex grips + `[N, 2N)` edge-midpoint grips with
  `type='midpoint'` + `edgeVertexIndices=[i, (i+1) % N]`). `applySlabOpeningGripDrag(gripKind, input)`
  dispatches by prefix: `slab-opening-vertex-N` вЖТ translate indexed vertex (XY,
  z preserved); `slab-opening-edge-midpoint-N` вЖТ insert fresh `Point3D` at
  `midpoint(verts[N], verts[(N+1) mod len]) + delta` (z averaged ѕМѕДќ±ќљ present).
  Out-of-range / unknown / zero-delta short-circuit. `rectilinear=true`
  quantizes delta ѕГѕДќњќљ dominant world axis (`|dx| вЙ• |dy|` вЖТ keep dx, drop dy).
- [x] `hooks/grip-types.ts` вАФ `SlabOpeningGripKind = \`slab-opening-vertex-${number}\` | \`slab-opening-edge-midpoint-${number}\``
  discriminated template-literal union + `GripInfo.slabOpeningGripKind?` field.
- [x] `hooks/useGripMovement.ts` вАФ re-export `SlabOpeningGripKind`.
- [x] `hooks/grips/unified-grip-types.ts` вАФ `UnifiedGripInfo.slabOpeningGripKind?` field.
- [x] `hooks/grips/grip-registry.ts` вАФ `wrapDxfGrip` forwards `slabOpeningGripKind` conditionally.
- [x] `hooks/grips/grip-parametric-commits.ts` вАФ `commitSlabOpeningGripDrag(grip, delta, deps)`:
  resolves opening via `sceneManager.getEntity`, reads `ShiftKeyTracker.getSnapshot()`
  ќ≥ќєќ± rectilinear, builds `UpdateSlabOpeningParamsCommand` ќЉќµ `isDragging=true`,
  emits `bim:slab-opening-params-updated`. Mirror ѕДќњѕЕ `commitSlabGripDrag`.
- [x] `hooks/grips/grip-commit-adapters.ts` вАФ `commitDxfGripDragModeAware`
  early-branches ѕГќµ `grip.slabOpeningGripKind` ѕАѕБќєќљ ѕДќ± stretch / move / rotate
  paths (mirror ѕДќњѕЕ slabGripKind branch).
- [x] `bim/renderers/SlabOpeningRenderer.ts` вАФ `getGrips(entity)` ѕАќїќ≠ќњќљ ќ≥ѕЕѕБќљќђ
  `getSlabOpeningGrips(entity).map(...)` ќ±ќљѕДќѓ ќ≥ќєќ± `[]` stub. `type='midpoint'`
  forwarding ќ≥ќєќ± edge-midpoint grips.
- [x] `bim/slab-openings/__tests__/slab-opening-grips.test.ts` вАФ 21 Jest tests
  (mirror ѕДќњѕЕ `slab-grips.test.ts` Phase 3.5+3.6): stable index order, vertex
  positions, type/movesEntity/entityId, degenerate polygon, per-vertex translate
  (preserve z, zero-delta + out-of-range short-circuit, unknown grip kind),
  edge-midpoint positions (incl. closing edge wrap), `type='midpoint'` +
  `edgeVertexIndices`, vertex insertion at `midpoint + delta` (length+1, original
  vertices untouched), closing-edge insertion, rectilinear quantization on each
  axis + tie-break + edge-midpoint interaction + default-off, foreign params
  preservation (kind / slabId / fireRating / elevationOverride / multiStoreyStackGroupId).
- [x] `bim/renderers/__tests__/SlabRenderer-with-slab-openings.test.ts` вАФ 6 Jest
  tests for the boolean cutout pass (no openings вЖТ no `destination-out`,
  registered opening вЖТ scoped destination-out, cutout outline filled, foreign
  slab id ignored, stroke survives, multi-opening per-opening cutout).

**Deferred to Phase 3.7b+:**
- [x] ~~Multi-storey stack group UI ("Copy to all floors")~~ **вЬЕ Phase 3.7b+ (2026-05-20)**: `SlabOpeningStackHost` + `SlabOpeningStackDialog` + ribbon `copyToFloors` action. EventBus decoupled. Enterprise ID `bmstkg`. `findHostSlabForLevel` + `buildStackedOpeningEntity` pure SSoT.
- [x] ~~Fire-rating in ribbon~~ **вЬЕ Phase 3.7b (2026-05-20)**: fireRating combobox (60/90/120/none) + i18n el+en. Material deferred to Phase 6.5.
- [x] ~~Snap-to-edge-midpoint preview ghost~~ **вЬЕ Phase 3.7b+ (2026-05-20)**: `useSlabOpeningGhostPreview` + `SlabOpeningGhostRenderer` вАФ rectangle ghost (dashed stroke + 25% fill + crosshair marker) at snapped cursor position. RAF pattern, micro-leaf ADR-040 compliant. `getImmediateSnap()` imperative read mirrors Phase 4.5c.4.

### Phase 3.8 вАФ Slab Vertex Editing (Add / Remove Corner) *(вЬЕ IMPLEMENTED 2026-05-22)*

Revit-style **Edit Boundary** vertex editing ќ≥ќєќ± existing slabs: hover corner grip вЖТ Delete key ќ±ѕЖќ±ќєѕБќµќѓ ќ≥ѕЙќљќѓќ±, right-click вЖТ context menu "Delete corner" / "Add corner here", min-3-vertex guard, undo/redo ќЉќ≠ѕГѕЙ `UpdateSlabParamsCommand`.

**Design choices:**
- **`hoveredDxfGrip` ѕЙѕВ Delete trigger** вАФ ќµќљѕДќњѕАќѓќґќµќє vertex grip ќЇќђѕДѕЙ ќ±ѕАѕМ cursor ќ±ќљѕДќѓ ќљќ± ќµѕАќµќЇѕДќµќѓќљќµќє ѕДќњ `SelectedGrip` overlay-only state. Zero state duplication, ќ±ќЇѕБќєќ≤ѕОѕВ ѕДќњ UX ѕАќњѕЕ ќ±ќљќ±ќЉќ≠ќљќµќє ќњ ѕЗѕБќЃѕГѕДќЈѕВ (hover + Delete).
- **Pure `removeVertexFromSlab()`** вАФ mirror ѕДќњѕЕ `applySlabGripDrag` pattern: ќіќ≠ѕЗќµѕДќ±ќє `SlabParams + vertexIndex`, ќµѕАќєѕГѕДѕБќ≠ѕЖќµќє ќљќ≠ќњ `SlabParams` ќЃ referentially ќѓќіќєќњ ќ±ќљ out-of-range / min-3 guard. Zero side effects.
- **Context menu dispatch ќЉќ≠ѕГѕЙ `getGlobalCommandHistory().execute()`** вАФ ќѓќіќєќњ pattern ќЉќµ session undo, ќ±ѕАќњѕЖќµѕНќ≥ќµќє ќљќ≠ќњ prop threading ќ±ѕАѕМ `CanvasSection`.
- **"Add corner here" ќ±ѕАѕМ context menu** вАФ ќЇќ±ќїќµќѓ `applySlabGripDrag(kind, {delta:{x:0,y:0}})` ѕАќњѕЕ ќµќєѕГќђќ≥ќµќє vertex ѕГѕДќњ ќ±ќЇѕБќєќ≤ќ≠ѕВ edge midpoint (zero delta = ќЇќ±ќЉќѓќ± ќЉќµѕДќ±ѕДѕМѕАќєѕГќЈ).

**Files created (0) / modified (8):**
- `bim/slabs/slab-grips.ts` вАФ ќљќ≠ќ± exported `removeVertexFromSlab(originalParams, vertexIndex)`: min-3 guard + out-of-range guard вЖТ referential short-circuit, ќ±ќїќїќєѕОѕВ `filter` ќ±ѕЖќ±ќєѕБќµќѓ ѕДќњќљ indexed vertex, spread preserves all other params.
- `bim/slabs/__tests__/slab-grips.test.ts` вАФ 5 ќљќ≠ќ± tests (20-24): remove indexed vertex (length 4вЖТ3), min-3 guard (triangle вЖТ identity), out-of-range ¬±index вЖТ identity, removing vertex-0 shifts remaining correctly, preserves kind/thickness/levelElevation. (Old test 20 вЖТ 25.)
- `hooks/canvas/useSmartDelete.ts` вАФ ќљќ≠ќњ `hoveredDxfGrip?: UnifiedGripInfo | null` ѕГѕДќњ Params interface. PRIORITY 0.5 block (ќµќЇѕДќµќїќµќѓѕДќ±ќє ѕАѕБќєќљ ѕДќњ PRIORITY 1 overlay vertex): ќ±ќљќєѕЗќљќµѕНќµќє `slab-vertex-*` grip kind, resolve entity via `LevelSceneManagerAdapter.getEntity`, `removeVertexFromSlab` + `UpdateSlabParamsCommand` + `executeCommand`.
- `hooks/canvas/useCanvasEditActions.ts` вАФ forward `hoveredDxfGrip` ќ±ѕАѕМ params ѕГќµ `useSmartDelete`.
- `components/dxf-layout/CanvasSection.tsx` вАФ ѕАќ≠ѕБќљќ±ќ≥ќµ `hoveredDxfGrip: unified.hoveredGrip` ѕГѕДќњ `useCanvasEditActions`.
- `systems/grip/grip-context-menu-resolver.ts` вАФ ќљќ≠ќ± `GripContextActionId` literals `'vertex-ops:deleteCorner' | 'vertex-ops:addCorner'`, ќљќ≠ќњ section id `'vertex-ops'`, `buildVertexOpsSection(grip)` pure builder ѕАќњѕЕ ќ±ќљќєѕЗќљќµѕНќµќє `slab-vertex-*` / `slab-edge-midpoint-*` / `slab-opening-*` kinds, `resolveContextMenuSections` ќіќ≠ѕЗќµѕДќ±ќє `grip` arg ќЇќ±ќє ќµќљќѓѕГѕЗќµќє ѕДќєѕВ sections.
- `systems/grip/grip-context-menu-actions.ts` вАФ ќљќ≠ќ± `onSlabVertexOp?` callback ѕГѕДќњ `GripContextActionBindContext`, `grip?: UnifiedGripInfo` 3ќњ arg ѕГѕДќњ `bindContextMenuAction`, 2 ќљќ≠ќ± cases `'vertex-ops:deleteCorner'` + `'vertex-ops:addCorner'` ѕГѕДќњ dispatch switch.
- `hooks/grips/useGripContextMenuController.ts` вАФ `LevelManagerLike` extended ќЉќµ `setLevelScene`, `onSlabVertexOp` callback (resolve entity вЖТ `removeVertexFromSlab` / `applySlabGripDrag` вЖТ `UpdateSlabParamsCommand` вЖТ `getGlobalCommandHistory().execute()`), pass `onSlabVertexOp` + `grip` ѕГѕДќњ `bindContextMenuAction`.
- `i18n/locales/en/tool-hints.json` + `i18n/locales/el/tool-hints.json` вАФ ќљќ≠ќ± keys `gripContextMenu.deleteCorner`, `gripContextMenu.addCorner`, `gripContextMenu.section.vertexOps`.
